Create an Animation with a duration and easing function\n+//   2. Call update(delta_ms) each tick to advance the animation\n+//   3. Use progress() or value() to get the current interpolated value\n+//   4. Check isComplete() to know when to stop\n+\n+const std = @import(\"std\");\n+\n+/// Easing functions for animation curves.\n+/// All functions map input [0.0, 1.0] to output [0.0, 1.0].\n+pub const Easing = enum {\n+    /// Constant velocity (no acceleration).\n+    linear,\n+\n+    /// Slow start, accelerating.\n+    ease_in,\n+\n+    /// Slow end, decelerating.\n+    ease_out,\n+\n+    /// Slow start and end.\n+    ease_in_out,\n+\n+    /// Quadratic ease in (t^2).\n+    quad_in,\n+\n+    /// Quadratic ease out.\n+    quad_out,\n+\n+    /// Quadratic ease in-out.\n+    quad_in_out,\n+\n+    /// Cubic ease in (t^3).\n+    cubic_in,\n+\n+    /// Cubic ease out.\n+    cubic_out,\n+\n+    /// Cubic ease in-out.\n+    cubic_in_out,\n+\n+    /// Elastic bounce at end.\n+    elastic_out,\n+\n+    /// Overshoot and settle back.\n+    back_out,\n+\n+    /// Multiple bounces at end.\n+    bounce_out,\n+\n+    /// Apply the easing function to a progress value [0.0, 1.0].\n+    pub fn apply(self: Easing, t: f32) f32 {\n+        const clamped = @min(1.0, @max(0.0, t));\n+        return switch (self) {\n+            .linear => clamped,\n+            .ease_in =>     .cubic_in_out => easeInOutCubic(clamped),\n+            .elastic_out => elasticOut(clamped),\n+            .back_out => backOut(clamped),\n+            .bounce_out => bounceOut(clamped),\n+        };\n+    }\n+\n+    fn easeInCubic(t: f32) f32 {\n+        return t * t * t;\n+    }\n+\n+    fn easeOutCubic(t: f32) f32 {\n+        const u = 1.0 - t;\n+        return 1.0 - u * u * u;\n+    }\n+\n+    fn easeInOutCubic(t: f32) f32 {\n+        if (t < 0.5) {\n+            return 4.0 * t * t * t;\n+        } else {\n+            const u = -2.0 * t + 2.0;\n+            return 1.0 - u * u * u / 2.0;\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    fn quadInOut(t: f32) f32 {\n+        if (t < 0.5) {\n+            return 2.0 * t * t;\n+        } else {\n+            return 1.0 - (-2.0 * t + 2.0) * (-2.0 * t + 2.0) / 2.0;\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    fn elasticOut(t: f32) f32 {\n+        if (t == 0.0) return 0.0;\n+        if (t == 1.0) return 1.0;\n+\n+        const c4 = (2.0 * std.math.pi) / 3.0;\n+        return std.math.pow(f32, 2.0, -10.0 * t) * @sin((t * 10.0 - 0.75) * c4) + 1.0;\n+    }\n+\n+    fn backOut(t: f32) f32 {\n+        const c1: f32 = 1.70158;\n+        const c3 = c1 + 1.0;\n+        const u = t - 1.0;\n+        return 1.0 + c3 * u * u * u + c1 * u * u;\n+    }\n+\n+    fn bounceOut(t: f32) f32 {\n+        const n1: f32 = 7.5625;\n+        const d1: f32 = 2.75;\n+\n+        if (t < 1.0 / d1) {\n+            return n1 * t * t;\n+        } else if (t < 2.0 / d1) {\n+            const adjusted = t - 1.5 / d1;\n+            return n1 * adjusted * adjusted + 0.75;\n+        } else if (t < 2.5 / d1) {\n+            const adjusted = t - 2.25 / d1;\n+            return n1 * adjusted * adjusted + 0.9375;\n+        } else {\n+            const adjusted = t - 2.625 / d1;\n+ /// Whether to loop the animation.\n+    looping: bool = false,\n+    /// Whether the animation is paused.\n+    paused: bool = false,\n+    /// Direction for ping-pong animations (true = forward).\n+    forward: bool = true,\n+\n+    /// Create a new animation with the given duration.\n+    pub fn init(duration_ms: u32) Animation {\n+        return .{ .duration_ms = duration_ms };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Create an animation with duration and easing.\n+    pub fn initWithEasing(duration_ms: u32, easing: Easing) Animation {\n+        return .{ .duration_ms = duration_ms, .easing = easing };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Update the animation by the given delta time.\n+    /// Returns true if the animation is still active.\n+    pub fn update(self: *Animation, delta_ms: u32) bool {\n+        if (self.paused) return !self.isComplete();\n+\n+        self.elapsed_ms +|= delta_ms;\n+\n+        if (self.looping and self.elapsed_ms >= self.duration_ms) {\n+            self.elapsed_ms = self.elapsed_ms % self.duration_ms;\n+        }\n+\n+        return !self.isComplete();\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Get the raw progress (0.0 to 1.0) without easing.\n+    pub fn rawProgress(self: Animation) f32 {\n+        if (self.duration_ms == 0) return 1.0;\n+        const raw_t = @as(f32, @floatFromInt(self.elapsed_ms)) /\n+            @as(f32, @floatFromInt(self.duration_ms));\n+        return @min(1.0, raw_t);\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Get the eased progress (0.0 to 1.0).\n+    pub fn progress(self: Animation) f32 {\n+        return self.easing.apply(self.rawProgress());\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Interpolate a value between start and end based on current progress.\n+    pub fn value(self: Animation, start: f32, end: f32) f32 {\n+        return lerp(start, end, self.progress());\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Interpolate an integer value between start and end.\n+    pub fn valueInt(self: Animation, start: i32, end: i32) i32 {\n+        const t = self.progress();\n+        const result = @as(f32, @floatFromInt(start)) * (1.0 - t) +\n+            @as(f32, @floatFromInt(end)) * t;\n+        return @intFromFloat(@round(result));\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Interpolate a u16 value (common for positions).\n+    pub fn valueU16(self: Animation, start: u16, end: u16) u16 {\n+        const t = self.progress();\n+        const s = @as(f32, @floatFromInt(start));\n+        const e = @as(f32, @floatFromInt(end));\n+        const result = s * (1.0 - t) + e * t;\n+        return @intFromFloat(@max(0.0, @round(result)));\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Check if the animation has completed.\n+    pub fn isComplete(self: Animation) bool {\n+        if (self.looping) return false;\n+        return self.elapsed_ms >= self.duration_ms;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Reset the animation to the beginning.\n+    pub fn reset(self: *Animation) void {\n+        self.elapsed_ms = 0;\n+        self.forward = true;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Pause the animation.\n+    pub fn pause(self: *Animation) void {\n+        self.paused = true;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Resume the animation.\n+    pub fn unpause(self: *Animation) void {\n+        self.paused = false;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Toggle pause state.\n+    pub fn togglePause(self: *Animation) void {\n+        self.paused = !self.paused;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Set the animation to loop.\n+    pub fn setLooping(self: *Animation, looping: bool) Animation {\n+        self.looping = looping;\n+        return self.*;\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+/// Keyframe for multi-step animations.\n+pub const Keyframe = struct {\n+    /// Value at this keyframe.\n+    value: f32,\n+    /// Time position (0.0 to 1.0).\n+    time: f32,\n+    /// Easing to use until next keyframe.\n+    easing: Easing = .linear,\n+};\n+\n+/// Multi-keyframe animation sequence.\n+pub fn KeyframeAnimation(comptime max_keyframes: usize) type {\n+    return struct {\n+        const Self = @This();\n+\n+        keyframes: [max_keyframes]Keyframe = undefined,\n+        count: usize = 0,\n+        duration_ms: u32,\n+        elapsed_ms: u32 = 0,\n+        looping: bool = false,\n+\n+        /// Create a new keyframe animation.\n+        pub fn init(duration_ms: u32) Self {\n+            return .{ .duration_ms = duration_ms };\n+        }\n+\n+        /// Add a keyframe at the specified time position.\n+        pub fn addKeyframe(self: *Self, time: f32, val: f32, ease: Easing) bool {\n+            if (self.count >= max_keyframes) return false;\n+            self.keyframes[self.count] = .{\n+                .time = time,\n+                .value = val,\n+                .easing = ease,\n+            };\n+            self.count += 1;\n+            return true;\n+        }\n+\n+        /// Update the animation.\n+        pub fn update(self: *Self, delta_ms: u32) bool {\n+            self.elapsed_ms +|= delta_ms;\n+\n+            if (self.looping and self.elapsed_ms >= self.duration_ms) {\n+                self.elapsed_ms = self.elapsed_ms % self.duration_ms;\n+            }\n+\n+            return !self.isComplete();\n+        }\n+\n+        /// Get the current interpolated value.\n+        pub fn value(self: Self) f32 {\n+            if (self.count == 0) return 0.0;\n+            if (self.count == 1) return self.keyframes[0].value;\n+\n+            const t = @as(f32, @floatFromInt(self.elapsed_ms)) /\n+                @as(f32, @floatFromInt(self.duration_ms));\n+            const clamped_t = @min(1.0, @max(0.0, t));\n+\n+            // Find surrounding keyframes\n+            var prev_idx: usize = 0;\n+            var next_idx: usize = 0;\n+            for (0..self.count) |i| {\n+                if (self.keyframes[i].time <= clamped_t) {\n+                    prev_idx = i;\n+                }\n+                if (self.keyframes[i].time >= clamped_t and next_idx == 0) {\n+                    next_idx = i;\n+                    break;\n+                }\n+            }\n+\n+            if (next_idx == 0) next_idx = self.count - 1;\n+            if (prev_idx == next_idx) return self.keyframes[prev_idx].value;\n+\n+            const prev = self.keyframes[prev_idx];\n+            const next = self.keyframes[next_idx];\n+\n+            // Calculate local progress between keyframes\n+            const time_range = next.time - prev.time;\n+            if (time_range == 0) return prev.value;\n+\n+            const local_t = (clamped_t - prev.time) / time_range;\n+            const eased_t = prev.easing.apply(local_t);\n+\n+            return lerp(prev.value, next.value, eased_t);\n+        }\n+\n+        /// Check if animation is complete.\n+        pub fn isComplete(self: Self) bool {\n+            if (self.looping) return false;\n+            return self.elapsed_ms >= self.duration_ms;\n+        }\n+\n+        /// Reset to beginning.\n+        pub fn reset(self: *Self) void {\n+            self.elapsed_ms = 0;\n+        }\n+    };\n+}\n+\n+/// Duration helper for converting time units.\n+pub const Duration = struct {\n+    ms: u32,\n+\n+    pub fn fromMs(ms: u32) Duration {\n+        return .{ .ms = ms };\n+    }\n+\n+    pub fn fromSeconds(seconds: f32) Duration {\n+        return .{ .ms = @intFromFloat(seconds * 1000.0) };\n+    }\n+\n+    pub fn fromFrames(frames: u32, fps: u32) Duration {\n+        if (fps == 0) return .{ .ms = 0 };\n+        return .{ .ms = (frames * 1000) / fps };\n+    }\n+\n+    pub fn toSeconds(self: Duration) f32 {\n+        return @as(f32, @floatFromInt(self.ms)) / 1000.0;\n+    }\n+\n+    pub fn toFrames(self: Duration, fps: u32) u32 {\n+        if (fps == 0) return 0;\n+        return (self.ms * fps) / 1000;\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+/// Frame rate tracker for consistent animation timing.\n+pub const FrameTimer = struct {\n+    target_fps: u32 = 60,\n+    frame_duration_ms: u32 = 16,\n+    accumulated_ms: u32 = 0,\n+    frame_count: u64 = 0,\n+\n+    /// Create a timer targeting the specified FPS.\n+    pub fn init(target_fps: u32) FrameTimer {\n+        const fps = if (target_fps == 0) 60 else target_fps;\n+        return .{\n+            .target_fps = fps,\n+            .frame_duration_ms = 1000 / fps,\n+        };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Update with elapsed time, returns number of frames to process.\n+    pub fn update(self: *FrameTimer, delta_ms: u32) u32 {\n+        self.accumulated_ms +|= delta_ms;\n+        const frames = self.accumulated_ms / self.frame_duration_ms;\n+        self.accumulated_ms = self.accumulated_ms % self.frame_duration_ms;\n+        self.frame_count +|= frames;\n+        return @intCast(frames);\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Get milliseconds per frame for this timer.\n+    pub fn msPerFrame(self: FrameTimer) u32 {\n+        return self.frame_duration_ms;\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+/// Linear interpolation between two values.\n+pub fn lerp(a: f32, b: f32, t: f32) f32 {\n+    return a + (b - a) * t;\n+}\n+\n+/// Inverse linear interpolation: find t given value between a and b.\n+pub fn inverseLerp(a: f32, b: f32, value: f32) f32 {\n+    if (a == b) return 0.0;\n+    return (value - a) / (b - a);\n+}\n+\n+/// Remap a value from one range to another.\n+pub fn remap(value: f32, in_min: f32, in_max: f32, out_min: f32, out_max: f32) f32 {\n+    const t = inverseLerp(in_min, in_max, value);\n+    return lerp(out_min, out_max, t);\n+}\n+\n+/// Smoothstep interpolation (smooth cubic Hermite).\n+pub fn smoothstep(edge0: f32, edge1: f32, x: f32) f32 {\n+    const t = @min(1.0, @max(0.0, (x - edge0) / (edge1 - edge0)));\n+    return t * t * (3.0 - 2.0 * t);\n+}\n+\n+/// Smoother step (quintic interpolation, zero second derivative at edges).\n+pub fn smootherstep(edge0: f32, edge1: f32, x: f32) f32 {\n+    const t = @min(1.0, @max(0.0, (x - edge0) / (edge1 - edge0)));\n+    return t * t * t * (t * (t * 6.0 - 15.0) + 10.0);\n+}\n+\n+// ============================================================\n+// SANITY TESTS - Basic animation construction\n+// ============================================================\n+\n+test \"sanity: Animation construction\" {\n+    const anim = Animation.init(1000);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u32, 1000), anim.duration_ms);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u32, 0), anim.elapsed_ms);\n+    try std.testing.expect(!anim.isComplete());\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: Animation with easing\" {\n+    const anim 100644\nindex 0000000..7a180a2\n--- /dev/null\n+++ b/src/graphics.zig\n@@ -0,0 +1,800 @@\n+// Terminal graphics protocol support for zithril TUI framework\n+// Provides detection and rendering for:\n+// - Sixel graphics (DEC VT340+, xterm, mlterm)\n+// - Kitty graphics protocol (kitty terminal)\n+// - iTerm2 inline images (iTerm2, WezTerm)\n+//\n+// Usage:\n+//   1. Detect terminal capabilities with GraphicsCapabilities.detect()\n+//   2. Check which protocol is supported\n+//   3. Use the appropriate encoder to generate escape sequences\n+//   4. Write sequences to terminal output\n+\n+const std = @import(\"std\");\n+const builtin = @import(\"builtin\");\n+\n+const is_windows = builtin.os.tag == .windows;\n+\n+/// Graphics protocol types supported by terminals.\n+pub const GraphicsProtocol = enum {\n+    /// No graphics support.\n+    none,\n+    /// Sixel graphics (VT340+, xterm -ti vt340).\n+    sixel,\n+    /// Kitty graphics protocol.\n+    kitty,\n+    /// iTerm2 inline images.\n+    iterm2,\n+\n+    /// Returns the display name of the protocol.\n+    pub fn name(self: GraphicsProtocol) []const u8 {\n+        return switch (self) {\n+            .none => \"none\",\n+            .sixel => \"Sixel\",\n+            .kitty => \"Kitty\",\n+            .iterm2 => \"iTerm2\",\n+        };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Returns the maximum theoretical resolution (protocol limit).\n+    pub fn maxResolution(self: GraphicsProtocol) struct { width: u32, height: u32 } {\n+        return switch (self) {\n+            .none => .{ .width = 0, .height = 0 },\n+            .sixel => .{ .width = 4096, .height = 4096 },\n+            .kitty => .{ .width = 10000, .height = 10000 },\n+            .iterm2 => .{ .width = 10000, .height = 10000 },\n+        };\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+/// Graphics capabilities detected at runtime.\n+pub const GraphicsCapabilities = struct {\n+    /// Best available protocol for this terminal.\n+    protocol: GraphicsProtocol = .none,\n+    /// Whether Sixel is supported.\n+    sixel: bool = false,\n+    /// Whether Kitty graphics protocol is supported.\n+    kitty: bool = false,\n+    /// Whether iTerm2 inline images are supported.\n+    iterm2: bool = false,\n+    /// Cell width in pixels (if known).\n+    cell_width_px: ?u16 = null,\n+    /// Cell height in pixels (if known).\n+    cell_height_px: ?u16 = null,\n+\n+    /// Detect graphics capabilities from environment.\n+    pub fn detect() GraphicsCapabilities {\n+        var caps = GraphicsCapabilities{};\n+\n+        // Check for Kitty\n+        if (getEnv(\"KITTY_WINDOW_ID\") != null) {\n+            caps.kitty = true;\n+            caps.protocol = .kitty;\n+        }\n+\n+        // Check for iTerm2\n+        if (getEnv(\"ITERM_SESSION_ID\") != null or getEnv(\"ITERM_PROFILE\") != null) {\n+            caps.iterm2 = true;\n+            if (caps.protocol == .none) caps.protocol = .iterm2;\n+        }\n+\n+        // Check for WezTerm (supports iTerm2 protocol)\n+        if (getEnv(\"WEZTERM_PANE\") != null or getEnv(\"WEZTERM_UNIX_SOCKET\") != null) {\n+            caps.iterm2 = true;\n+            caps.kitty = true;\n+            if (caps.protocol == .none) caps.protocol = .kitty;\n+        }\n+\n+        // Check TERM for sixel hints\n+        if (getEnv(\"TERM\")) |term| {\n+            if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, term, \"sixel\") != null or\n+                std.mem.indexOf(u8, term, \"vt340\") != null)\n+            {\n+                caps.sixel = true;\n+                if (caps.protocol == .none) caps.protocol = .sixel;\n+            }\n+\n+            if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"xterm\")) {\n+                caps.sixel = true;\n+                if (caps.protocol == .none) caps.protocol = .sixel;\n+            }\n+\n+            if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"mlterm\")) {\n+                caps.sixel = true;\n+                if (caps.protocol == .none) caps.protocol = .sixel;\n+            }\n+        }\n+\n+        // Check for explicit sixel support\n+        if (getEnv(\"SIXEL_SUPPORT\") != null) {\n+            caps.sixel = true;\n+            if (caps.protocol == .none) caps.protocol = .sixel;\n+        }\n+\n+        return caps;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Check if any graphics protocol is available.\n+    pub fn hasGraphics(self: GraphicsCapabilities) bool {\n+        return self.protocol != .none;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Get the best available protocol.\n+    pub fn bestProtocol(self: GraphicsCapabilities) GraphicsProtocol {\n+        return self.protocol;\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+/// Sixel graphics encoder.\n+/// Converts pixel data to Sixel escape sequences.\n+pub const SixelEncoder = struct {\n+    /// Color palette (up to 256 colors for standard Sixel).\n+    palette: [256]RGB = undefined,\n+    palette_size: u8 = 0,\n+    /// Use private color registers (better color accuracy).\n+    use_private_colors: bool = true,\n+    /// Aspect ratio hint.\n+    aspect_ratio: u8 = 1,\n+\n+    pub const RGB = struct {\n+        r: u8,\n+        g: u8,\n+        b: u8,\n+\n+        pub fn init(r: u8, g: u8, b: u8) RGB {\n+            return .{ .r = r, .g = g, .b = b };\n+        }\n+\n+        pub fn toSixelPercent(self: RGB) struct { r: u8, g: u8, b: u8 } {\n+            return .{\n+                .r = @intCast((@as(u16, self.r) * 100) / 255),\n+                .g = @intCast((@as(u16, self.g) * 100) / 255),\n+                .b = @intCast((@as(u16, self.b) * 100) / 255),\n+            };\n+        }\n+    };\n+\n+    /// Create a new Sixel encoder with default palette.\n+    pub fn init() SixelEncoder {\n+        var encoder = SixelEncoder{};\n+        encoder.initDefaultPalette();\n+        return encoder;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Initialize with a basic 16-color palette.\n+    pub fn initDefaultPalette(self: *SixelEncoder) void {\n+        const colors = [_]RGB{\n+            RGB.init(0, 0, 0), // Black\n+            RGB.init(128, 0, 0), // Maroon\n+            RGB.init(0, 128, 0), // Green\n+            RGB.init(128, 128, 0), // Olive\n+            RGB.init(0, 0, 128), // Navy\n+            RGB.init(128, 0, 128), // Purple\n+            RGB.init(0, 128, 128), // Teal\n+            RGB.init(192, 192, 192), // Silver\n+            RGB.init(128, 128, 128), // Gray\n+            RGB.init(255, 0, 0), // Red\n+            RGB.init(0, 255, 0), // Lime\n+            RGB.init(255, 255, 0), // Yellow\n+            RGB.init(0, 0, 255), // Blue\n+            RGB.init(255, 0, 255), // Fuchsia\n+            RGB.init(0, 255, 255), // Aqua\n+            RGB.init(255, 255, 255), // White\n+        };\n+\n+        for (colors, 0..) |c, i| {\n+            self.palette[i] = c;\n+        }\n+        self.palette_size = 16;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Add a color to the palette.\n+    pub fn addColor(self: *SixelEncoder, color: RGB) ?u8 {\n+        if (self.palette_size >= 255) return null;\n+        self.palette[self.palette_size] = color;\n+        self.palette_size += 1;\n+        return self.palette_size - 1;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Find the closest color in the palette.\n+    pub fn findClosestColor(self: SixelEncoder, target: RGB) u8 {\n+        var best_idx: u8 = 0;\n+        var best_dist: u32 = std.math.maxInt(u32);\n+\n+        for (0..self.palette_size) |i| {\n+            const c = self.palette[i];\n+            const dr = @as(i32, target.r) - @as(i32, c.r);\n+            const dg = @as(i32, target.g) - @as(i32, c.g);\n+            const db = @as(i32, target.b) - @as(i32, c.b);\n+            const dist: u32 = @intCast(dr * dr + dg * dg + db * db);\n+\n+            if (dist < best_dist) {\n+                best_dist = dist;\n+                best_idx = @intCast(i);\n+            }\n+        }\n+\n+        return best_idx;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Write the Sixel header escape sequence.\n+    pub fn writeHeader(self: SixelEncoder, writer: anytype) !void {\n+        // DCS (Device Control String) for Sixel\n+        // Format: ESC P <params> q\n+        // params: P1;P2;P3 where P1=aspect ratio, P2=unused, P3=horizontal grid\n+        const p3: u8 = if (self.use_private_colors) 0 else 1;\n+        try writer.print(\"\\x1bP{d};{d};{d}q\", .{ self.aspect_ratio, 0, p3 });\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Write a color definition.\n+    pub fn writeColorDef(self: SixelEncoder, writer: anytype, idx: u8) !void {\n+        if (idx >= self.palette_size) return;\n+        const c = self.palette[idx];\n+        const pct = c.toSixelPercent();\n+        // Color definition: #<idx>;2;<r>;<g>;<b>\n+        // 2 = RGB color space\n+        try writer.print(\"#{d};2;{d};{d};{d}\", .{ idx, pct.r, pct.g, pct.b });\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Write all color definitions.\n+    pub fn writeAllColorDefs(self: SixelEncoder, writer: anytype) !void {\n+        for (0..self.palette_size) |i| {\n+            try self.writeColorDef(writer, @intCast(i));\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Write the Sixel footer (String Terminator).\n+    pub fn writeFooter(_: SixelEncoder, writer: anytype) !void {\n+        try writer.writeAll(\"\\x1b\\\\\");\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Encode a row of sixels (6 vertical pixels).\n+    /// Returns the sixel character for a 6-pixel column.\n+    pub fn encodeSixel(bitmap: u6) u8 {\n+        return @as(u8, bitmap) + 63;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Get escape sequence for selecting a color.\n+    pub fn selectColor(_: SixelEncoder, writer: anytype, idx: u8) !void {\n+        try writer.print(\"#{d}\", .{idx});\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Write a graphics new line (move down 6 pixels).\n+    pub fn writeNewLine(_: SixelEncoder, writer: anytype) !void {\n+        try writer.writeByte('-');\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Write a carriage return (move to start of current row).\n+    pub fn writeCR(_: SixelEncoder, writer: anytype) !void {\n+        try writer.writeByte('$');\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+/// Kitty graphics protocol encoder.\n+/// Supports direct pixel data and image references.\n+pub const KittyEncoder = struct {\n+    /// Image format.\n+    pub const Format = enum(u8) {\n+        /// 24-bit RGB.\n+        rgb = 24,\n+        /// 32-bit RGBA.\n+        rgba = 32,\n+        /// PNG data.\n+        png = 100,\n+    };\n+\n+    /// Transmission type.\n+    pub const Transmission = enum(u8) {\n+        /// Direct data in escape sequence.\n+        direct = 'd',\n+        /// File path.\n+        file = 'f',\n+        /// Temporary file path.\n+        temp_file = 't',\n+        /// Shared memory.\n+        shared_memory = 's',\n+    };\n+\n+    /// Action to perform.\n+    pub const Action = enum(u8) {\n+        /// Transmit data.\n+        transmit = 't',\n+        /// Transmit and display.\n+        transmit_display = 'T',\n+        /// Query terminal.\n+        query = 'q',\n+        /// Display previously transmitted.\n+        display = 'p',\n+        /// Delete images.\n+        delete = 'd',\n+        /// Animate frames.\n+        animate = 'a',\n+        /// Compose frames.\n+        compose = 'c',\n+    };\n+\n+    /// Image ID counter.\n+    next_id: u32 = 1,\n+\n+    pub fn init() KittyEncoder {\n+        return .{};\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Generate a unique image ID.\n+    pub fn nextImageId(self: *KittyEncoder) u32 {\n+        const id = self.next_id;\n+        self.next_id +|= 1;\n+        return id;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Write the start of a Kitty graphics command.\n+    pub fn writeCommandStart(writer: anytype, action: Action) !void {\n+        try writer.print(\"\\x1b_Ga={c}\", .{@intFromEnum(action)});\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Write an image transmission command.\n+    pub fn writeTransmit(\n+        writer: anytype,\n+        image_id: u32,\n+        format: Format,\n+        width: u32,\n+        height: u32,\n+        more_data: bool,\n+    ) !void {\n+        try writer.print(\"\\x1b_Ga=t,i={d},f={d},s={d},v={d}\", .{\n+            image_id,\n+            @intFromEnum(format),\n+            width,\n+            height,\n+        });\n+        if (more_data) {\n+            try writer.writeAll(\",m=1\");\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Write a display command.\n+    pub fn writeDisplay(\n+        writer: anytype,\n+        image_id: u32,\n+        x: u32,\n+        y: u32,\n+        cols: ?u32,\n+        rows: ?u32,\n+    ) !void {\n+        try writer.print(\"\\x1b_Ga=p,i={d},x={d},y={d}\", .{ image_id, x, y });\n+        if (cols) |c| {\n+            try writer.print(\",c={d}\", .{c});\n+        }\n+        if (rows) |r| {\n+            try writer.print(\",r={d}\", .{r});\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Write a delete command.\n+    pub fn writeDelete(writer: anytype, image_id: ?u32) !void {\n+        if (image_id) |id| {\n+            try writer.print(\"\\x1b_Ga=d,d=i,i={d}\", .{id});\n+        } else {\n+            try writer.writeAll(\"\\x1b_Ga=d,d=a\");\n+        }\n+        try writeCommandEnd(writer);\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Write base64-encoded data chunk.\n+    pub fn writeDataChunk(writer: anytype, data: []const u8, is_last: bool) !void {\n+        try writer.writeAll(\";\");\n+        try writeBase64(writer, data);\n+        if (!is_last) {\n+            try writer.writeAll(\",m=1\");\n+        }\n+        try writeCommandEnd(writer);\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Write command terminator.\n+    pub fn writeCommandEnd(writer: anytype) !void {\n+        try writer.writeAll(\"\\x1b\\\\\");\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+/// iTerm2 inline image protocol encoder.\n+pub const ITerm2Encoder = struct {\n+    /// Image options.\n+    pub const Options = struct {\n+        /// Width in cells (or auto if null).\n+        width: ?u32 = null,\n+        /// Height in cells (or auto if null).\n+        height: ?u32 = null,\n+        /// Preserve aspect ratio.\n+        preserve_aspect: bool = true,\n+        /// Whether image is inline (vs. download).\n+        inline_image: bool = true,\n+        /// Name for the image (optional).\n+        name: ?[]const u8 = null,\n+    };\n+\n+    pub fn init() ITerm2Encoder {\n+        return .{};\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Write an inline image command.\n+    pub fn writeImage(\n+        writer: anytype,\n+        data: []const u8,\n+        options: Options,\n+    ) !void {\n+        // OSC 1337 ; File=<args> : <base64 data> BEL\n+        try writer.writeAll(\"\\x1b]1337;File=\");\n+\n+        // Write options\n+        var first = true;\n+\n+        if (options.name) |n| {\n+            try writeParam(writer, &first, \"name\", n);\n+        }\n+\n+        if (options.width) |w| {\n+            try writeNumParam(writer, &first, \"width\", w);\n+        }\n+\n+        if (options.height) |h| {\n+            try writeNumParam(writer, &first, \"height\", h);\n+        }\n+\n+        if (options.preserve_aspect) {\n+            try writeFlagParam(writer, &first, \"preserveAspectRatio\", true);\n+        }\n+\n+        if (options.inline_image) {\n+            try writeFlagParam(writer, &first, \"inline\", true);\n+        }\n+\n+        try writer.writeAll(\":\");\n+\n+        // Write base64-encoded data\n+        try writeBase64(writer, data);\n+\n+        // Terminate with BEL\n+        try writer.writeByte(0x07);\n+    }\n+\n+    fn writeParam(writer: anytype, first: *bool, key: []const u8, value: []const u8) !void {\n+        if (!first.*) try writer.writeByte(';');\n+        first.* = false;\n+        try writer.writeAll(key);\n+        try writer.writeByte('=');\n+        try writer.writeAll(value);\n+    }\n+\n+    fn writeNumParam(writer: anytype, first: *bool, key: []const u8, value: u32) !void {\n+        if (!first.*) try writer.writeByte(';');\n+        first.* = false;\n+        try writer.writeAll(key);\n+        try writer.print(\"={d}\", .{value});\n+    }\n+\n+    fn writeFlagParam(writer: anytype, first: *bool, key: []const u8, value: bool) !void {\n+        if (!first.*) try writer.writeByte(';');\n+        first.* = false;\n+        try writer.writeAll(key);\n+        try writer.print(\"={d}\", .{@as(u8, if (value) 1 else 0)});\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+/// Base64 encoding table.\n+const base64_chars = \"ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789+/\";\n+\n+/// Write base64-encoded data to writer.\n+fn writeBase64(writer: anytype, data: []const u8) !void {\n+    var i: usize = 0;\n+    while (i + 3 <= data.len) : (i += 3) {\n+        const b0 = data[i];\n+        const b1 = data[i + 1];\n+        const b2 = data[i + 2];\n+\n+        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[b0 >> 2]);\n+        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[((b0 & 0x03) << 4) | (b1 >> 4)]);\n+        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[((b1 & 0x0F) << 2) | (b2 >> 6)]);\n+        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[b2 & 0x3F]);\n+    }\n+\n+    const remaining = data.len - i;\n+    if (remaining == 1) {\n+        const b0 = data[i];\n+        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[b0 >> 2]);\n+        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[(b0 & 0x03) << 4]);\n+        try writer.writeAll(\"==\");\n+    } else if (remaining == 2) {\n+        const b0 = data[i];\n+        const b1 = data[i + 1];\n+        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[b0 >> 2]);\n+        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[((b0 & 0x03) << 4) | (b1 >> 4)]);\n+        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[(b1 & 0x0F) << 2]);\n+        try writer.writeByte('=');\n+    }\n+}\n+\n+/// Cross-platform environment variable getter.\n+fn getEnv(name: []const u8) ?[]const u8 {\n+    if (is_windows) {\n+        return std.process.getEnvVarOwned(std.heap.page_allocator, name) catch null;\n+    } else {\n+        return std.posix.getenv(name);\n+    }\n+}\n+\n+// b/src/widgets/scroll_view.zig\nnew file mode 100644\nindex 0000000..55be7ae\n--- /dev/null\n+++ b/src/widgets/scroll_view.zig\n@@ -0,0 +1,940 @@\n+// ScrollView widget for zithril TUI framework\n+// Virtual scrolling container with scroll state management and scrollbar integration\n+\n+const std = @import(\"std\");\n+const buffer_mod = @import(\"../buffer.zig\");\n+const geometry = @import(\"../geometry.zig\");\n+const style_mod = @import(\"../style.zig\");\n+const scrollbar_mod = @import(\"scrollbar.zig\");\n+const event_mod = @import(\"../event.zig\");\n+\n+pub const Buffer = buffer_mod.Buffer;\n+pub const Cell = buffer_mod.Cell;\n+pub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\n+pub const Style = style_mod.Style;\n+pub const Scrollbar = scrollbar_mod.Scrollbar;\n+pub const Orientation = scrollbar_mod.Orientation;\n+pub const MouseKind = event_mod.MouseKind;\n+pub const Mouse = event_mod.Mouse;\n+pub const KeyCode = event_mod.KeyCode;\n+pub const Key = event_mod.Key;\n+\n+/// Scroll state for a scrollable container.\n+/// Tracks scroll position and provides helpers for navigation.\n+pub const ScrollState = struct {\n+    /// Current vertical scroll offset (first visible row).\n+    offset: usize = 0,\n+\n+    /// Total number of items/rows in the content.\n+    total: usize = 0,\n+\n+    /// Viewport height (number of visible rows).\n+    viewport: u16 = 0,\n+\n+    /// Create a new scroll state.\n+    pub fn init(total: usize) ScrollState {\n+        return .{ .total = total };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Update viewport size and clamp offset if needed.\n+    pub fn setViewport(self: *ScrollState, viewport: u16) void {\n+        self.viewport = viewport;\n+        self.clampOffset();\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Update total content size and clamp offset if needed.\n+    pub fn setTotal(self: *ScrollState, total: usize) void {\n+        self.total = total;\n+        self.clampOffset();\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Scroll to a specific offset (clamped to valid range).\n+    pub fn scrollTo(self: *ScrollState, offset: usize) void {\n+        self.offset = offset;\n+        self.clampOffset();\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Scroll by a delta amount (positive = down, negative = up).\n+    pub fn scrollBy(self: *ScrollState, delta: i32) void {\n+        if (delta < 0) {\n+            const abs_delta: usize = @intCast(-delta);\n+            self.offset -|= abs_delta;\n+        } else {\n+            const pos_delta: usize = @intCast(delta);\n+            self.offset +|= pos_delta;\n+        }\n+        self.clampOffset();\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Scroll up by one line.\n+    pub fn scrollUp(self: *ScrollState) void {\n+        self.scrollBy(-1);\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Scroll down by one line.\n+    pub fn scrollDown(self: *ScrollState) void {\n+        self.scrollBy(1);\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Scroll up by one page (viewport height).\n+    pub fn pageUp(self: *ScrollState) void {\n+        self.scrollBy(-@as(i32, @intCast(self.viewport)));\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Scroll down by one page (viewport height).\n+    pub fn pageDown(self: *ScrollState) void {\n+        self.scrollBy(@as(i32, @intCast(self.viewport)));\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Scroll to the beginning.\n+    pub fn scrollToStart(self: *ScrollState) void {\n+        self.offset = 0;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Scroll to the end.\n+    pub fn scrollToEnd(self: *ScrollState) void {\n+        self.offset = self.maxOffset();\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Ensure a specific index is visible, scrolling if necessary.\n+    pub fn ensureVisible(self: *ScrollState, index: usize) void {\n+        if (index < self.offset) {\n+            self.offset = index;\n+        } else if (index >= self.offset + self.viewport) {\n+            self.offset = index -| (self.viewport -| 1);\n+        }\n+        self.clampOffset();\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Get the maximum valid scroll offset.\n+    pub fn maxOffset(self: ScrollState) usize {\n+        if (self.total <= self.viewport) return 0;\n+        return self.total - self.viewport;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Check if currently at the top.\n+    pub fn atStart(self: ScrollState) bool {\n+        return self.offset == 0;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Check if currently at the bottom.\n+    pub fn atEnd(self: ScrollState) bool {\n+        return self.offset >= self.maxOffset();\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Check if scrolling is needed (content exceeds viewport).\n+    pub fn canScroll(self: ScrollState) bool {\n+        return self.total > self.viewport;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Get the range of visible indices [start, end).\n+    pub fn visibleRange(self: ScrollState) struct { start: usize, end: usize } {\n+        const start = self.offset;\n+        const end = @min(self.offset + self.viewport, self.total);\n+        return .{ .start = start, .end = end };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Clamp offset to valid range.\n+    fn clampOffset(self: *ScrollState) void {\n+        self.offset = @min(self.offset, self.maxOffset());\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Handle keyboard input for scrolling.\n+    /// Returns true if the event was handled.\n+    pub fn handleKey(self: *ScrollState, key: Key) bool {\n+        switch (key.code) {\n+            .up => {\n+                self.scrollUp();\n+                return true;\n+            },\n+            .down => {\n+                self.scrollDown();\n+                return true;\n+            },\n+            .page_up => {\n+                self.pageUp();\n+                return true;\n+            },\n+            .page_down => {\n+                self.pageDown();\n+                return true;\n+            },\n+            .home => if (key.modifiers.ctrl) {\n+                self.scrollToStart();\n+                return true;\n+            },\n+            .end => if (key.modifiers.ctrl) {\n+                self.scrollToEnd();\n+                return true;\n+            },\n+            else => {},\n+        }\n+        return false;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Handle mouse scroll events.\n+    /// Returns true if the event was handled.\n+    pub fn handleMouse(self: *ScrollState, mouse: Mouse) bool {\n+        switch (mouse.kind) {\n+            .scroll_up => {\n+                self.scrollBy(-3);\n+                return true;\n+            },\n+            .scroll_down => {\n+                self.scrollBy(3);\n+                return true;\n+            },\n+            else => {},\n+        }\n+        return false;\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+/// ScrollView widget configuration.\n+/// Wraps content with virtual scrolling and optional scrollbar.\n+pub const ScrollView = struct {\n+    /// Scroll state (tracks position).\n+    state: *ScrollState,\n+\n+    /// Show scrollbar when content exceeds viewport.\n+    show_scrollbar: bool = true,\n+\n+    /// Scrollbar style.\n+    scrollbar_style: Style = Style.empty,\n+\n+    /// Scrollbar thumb style.\n+    scrollbar_thumb_style: Style = Style.init().reverse(),\n+\n+    /// Background style for the viewport.\n+    style: Style = Style.empty,\n+\n+    /// Scrollbar position (right edge by default).\n+    scrollbar_on_left: bool = false,\n+\n+    /// Get the content area (viewport minus scrollbar if shown).\n+    pub fn contentArea(self: ScrollView, area: Rect) Rect {\n+        if (!self.show_scrollbar or !self.state.canScroll()) {\n+            return area;\n+        }\n+\n+        if (self.scrollbar_on_left) {\n+            return Rect.init(\n+                area.x +| 1,\n+                area.y,\n+                area.width -| 1,\n+                area.height,\n+            );\n+        } else {\n+            return Rect.init(\n+                area.x,\n+                area.y,\n+                area.width -| 1,\n+                area.height,\n+            );\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Get the scrollbar area.\n+    pub fn scrollbarArea(self: ScrollView, area: Rect) Rect {\n+        if (self.scrollbar_on_left) {\n+            return Rect.init(area.x, area.y, 1, area.height);\n+        } else {\n+            return Rect.init(area.x +| (area.width -| 1), area.y, 1, area.height);\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Render the scrollbar (if needed).\n+    pub fn render(self: ScrollView, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n+        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n+\n+        // Update viewport in scroll state\n+        self.state.setViewport(area.height);\n+\n+        // Fill background\n+        if (!self.style.isEmpty()) {\n+            buf.fill(area, Cell.styled(' ', self.style));\n+        }\n+\n+        // Draw scrollbar if needed\n+        if (self.show_scrollbar and self.state.canScroll()) {\n+            const sb_area = self.scrollbarArea(area);\n+            const scrollbar = Scrollbar{\n+                .total = self.state.total,\n+                .position = self.state.offset,\n+                .viewport = self.state.viewport,\n+                .style = self.scrollbar_style,\n+                .thumb_style = self.scrollbar_thumb_style,\n+                .orientation = .vertical,\n+            };\n+            scrollbar.render(sb_area, buf);\n+        }\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+/// ScrollableList combines List behavior with virtual scrolling.\n+/// Renders only visible items and integrates with ScrollState.\n+pub const ScrollableList = struct {\n+    /// Items to display.\n+    items: []const []const u8,\n+\n+    /// Scroll state.\n+    scroll: *ScrollState,\n+\n+    /// Currently selected item index (null for no selection).\n+    selected: ?usize = null,\n+\n+    /// Default style for non-selected items.\n+    style: Style = Style.empty,\n+\n+    /// Style for the selected item.\n+    highlight_style: Style = Style.init().bg(.blue),\n+\n+    /// Prefix shown before the selected item.\n+    highlight_symbol: []const u8 = \"> \",\n+\n+    /// Show scrollbar when content exceeds viewport.\n+    show_scrollbar: bool = true,\n+\n+    /// Scrollbar style.\n+    scrollbar_style: Style = Style.empty,\n+\n+    /// Scrollbar thumb style.\n+    scrollbar_thumb_style: Style = Style.init().reverse(),\n+\n+    /// Update scroll state from items.\n+    pub fn syncState(self: *ScrollableList) void {\n+        self.scroll.setTotal(self.items.len);\n+        if (self.selected) |sel| {\n+            self.scroll.ensureVisible(sel);\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Move selection up.\n+    pub fn selectPrevious(self: *ScrollableList) void {\n+        if (self.items.len == 0) return;\n+        if (self.selected) |sel| {\n+            if (sel > 0) {\n+                self.selected = sel - 1;\n+                self.scroll.ensureVisible(sel - 1);\n+            }\n+        } else {\n+            self.selected = 0;\n+            self.scroll.ensureVisible(0);\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Move selection down.\n+    pub fn selectNext(self: *ScrollableList) void {\n+        if (self.items.len == 0) return;\n+        if (self.selected) |sel| {\n+            if (sel + 1 < self.items.len) {\n+                self.selected = sel + 1;\n+                self.scroll.ensureVisible(sel + 1);\n+            }\n+        } else {\n+            self.selected = 0;\n+            self.scroll.ensureVisible(0);\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Select first item.\n+    pub fn selectFirst(self: *ScrollableList) void {\n+        if (self.items.len == 0) return;\n+        self.selected = 0;\n+        self.scroll.ensureVisible(0);\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Select last item.\n+    pub fn selectLast(self: *ScrollableList) void {\n+        if (self.items.len == 0) return;\n+        self.selected = self.items.len - 1;\n+        self.scroll.ensureVisible(self.items.len - 1);\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Handle keyboard input for navigation.\n+    /// Returns true if the event was handled.\n+    pub fn handleKey(self: *ScrollableList, key: Key) bool {\n+        switch (key.code) {\n+            .up => {\n+                self.selectPrevious();\n+                return true;\n+            },\n+            .down => {\n+                self.selectNext();\n+                return true;\n+            },\n+            .home => {\n+                self.selectFirst();\n+                return true;\n+            },\n+            .end => {\n+                self.selectLast();\n+                return true;\n+            },\n+            .page_up => {\n+                if (self.items.len == 0) return true;\n+                if (self.selected) |sel| {\n+                    const page = self.scroll.viewport;\n+                    self.selected = sel -| page;\n+                    self.scroll.ensureVisible(self.selected.?);\n+                }\n+                return true;\n+            },\n+            .page_down => {\n+                if (self.items.len == 0) return true;\n+                if (self.selected) |sel| {\n+                    const page = self.scroll.viewport;\n+                    self.selected = @min(sel + page, self.items.len -| 1);\n+                    self.scroll.ensureVisible(self.selected.?);\n+                }\n+                return true;\n+            },\n+            else => {},\n+        }\n+        return false;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Render the scrollable list.\n+    pub fn render(self: ScrollableList, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n+        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n+\n+        // Calculate content area (minus scrollbar if needed)\n+        const needs_scrollbar = self.show_scrollbar and self.items.len > area.height;\n+        const content_width = if (needs_scrollbar) area.width -| 1 else area.width;\n+        const content_area = Rect.init(area.x, area.y, content_width, area.height);\n+\n+        if (content_area.isEmpty()) return;\n+\n+        const symbol_len: u16 = @intCast(@min(self.highlight_symbol.len, content_area.width));\n+        const content_start = content_area.x +| symbol_len;\n+        const text_width = content_area.width -| symbol_len;\n+\n+        // Get visible range\n+        const range = self.scroll.visibleRange();\n+\n+        // Render visible items\n+        var y = content_area.y;\n+        var item_index = range.start;\n+        while (item_index < range.end and y < content_area.bottom()) : ({\n+            y += 1;\n+            item_index += 1;\n+        }) {\n+            const item = self.items[item_index];\n+            const is_selected = self.selected != null and self.selected.? == item_index;\n+\n+            if (is_selected) {\n+                // Fill the entire row with highlight style\n+                const row_rect = Rect.init(content_area.x, y, content_area.width, 1);\n+                buf.fill(row_rect, Cell.styled(' ', self.highlight_style));\n+\n+                // Draw highlight symbol\n+                if (symbol_len > 0) {\n+                    buf.setString(content_area.x, y, self.highlight_symbol[0..symbol_len], self.highlight_style);\n+                }\n+\n+                // Draw item text with highlight style\n+                if (text_width > 0) {\n+                    buf.setString(content_start, y, item, self.highlight_style);\n+                }\n+            } else {\n+                // Draw item text with normal style\n+                if (text_width > 0) {\n+                    buf.setString(content_start, y, item, self.style);\n+                }\n+            }\n+        }\n+\n+        // Draw scrollbar if needed\n+        if (needs_scrollbar) {\n+            const sb_area = Rect.init(area.x +| content_width, area.y, 1, area.height);\n+            const scrollbar = Scrollbar{\n+                .total = self.items.len,\n+                .position = self.scroll.offset,\n+                .viewport = area.height,\n+                .style = self.scrollbar_style,\n+                .thumb_style = self.scrollbar_thumb_style,\n+                .orientation = .vertical,\n+            };\n+            scrollbar.render(sb_area, buf);\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Get the number of items.\n+    pub fn len(self: ScrollableList) usize {\n+        return self.items.len;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Check if empty.\n+    pub fn isEmpty(self: ScrollableList) bool {\n+        return self.items.len == 0;\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+// ============================================================\n+// SANITY TESTS - ScrollState basic functionality\n+// ============================================================\n+\n+test \"sanity: ScrollState default values\" {\n+    const state = ScrollState{};\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), state.offset);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), state.total);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 0), state.viewport);\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: ScrollState.init\" {\n+    const ScrollState.setViewport\" {\n+    var state = ScrollState.init(100);\n+    state.setViewport(20);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 20), state.viewport);\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: state.offset);\n+\n+    state.scrollBy(-100);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), state.offset);\n+\n+    state.scrollBy(200);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 80), state.offset);\n+}\n+\n+test \"behavior: ScrollState.pageUp and pageDown\" {\n+    var state = ScrollState.init(100);\n+    state.setViewport(20);\n+\n+    state.scrollTo(50);\n+    state.pageUp();\n+ std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 40), state.offset);\n+\n+    // Item below viewport\n+    state.ensureVisible(80);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 61), state.offset);\n+}\n+\n+test zithril TUI framework\n+// Single-line text input with cursor movement, selection, and clipboard support\n+\n+const std = @import(\"std\");\n+const buffer_mod = @import(\"../buffer.zig\");\n+const geometry = @import(\"../geometry.zig\");\n+const style_mod = @import(\"../style.zig\");\n+const event_mod = @import(\"../event.zig\");\n+\n+pub const Buffer = buffer_mod.Buffer;\n+pub const Cell = buffer_mod.Cell;\n+pub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\n+pub const Style = style_mod.Style;\n+pub const Key = event_mod.Key;\n+pub const KeyCode = event_mod.KeyCode;\n+pub const Modifiers = event_mod.Modifiers;\n+\n+/// Text input state managing content, cursor, and selection.\n+pub const TextInputState = struct {\n+    /// The text content (user provides backing storage).\n+    buffer: []u8,\n+\n+    /// Current length of text content.\n+    len: usize = 0,\n+\n+    /// Cursor position (byte index).\n+    cursor: usize = 0,\n+\n+    /// Selection anchor (byte index). If different from cursor, text is selected.\n+    /// Selection range is [min(anchor, cursor), max(anchor, cursor)).\n+    anchor: usize = 0,\n+\n+    /// Horizontal scroll offset (for text wider than viewport).\n+    scroll_offset: usize = 0,\n+\n+    /// Maximum allowed content length (0 = use buffer size).\n+    max_len: usize = 0,\n+\n+    /// Create a new text input state with the given buffer.\n+    pub fn init(backing_buffer: []u8) TextInputState {\n+        return .{\n+            .buffer = backing_buffer,\n+        };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Create a text input state with initial content.\n+    pub fn initWithContent(backing_buffer: []u8, initial: []const u8) TextInputState {\n+        var state = init(backing_buffer);\n+        state.setText(initial);\n+        return state;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Get the current text content.\n+    pub fn text(self: TextInputState) []const u8 {\n+        return self.buffer[0..self.len];\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Set the text content, replacing all existing content.\n+    pub fn setText(self: *TextInputState, content: []const u8) void {\n+        const max = self.maxLength();\n+        const copy_len = @min(content.len, max);\n+        @memcpy(self.buffer[0..copy_len], content[0..copy_len]);\n+        self.len = copy_len;\n+        self.cursor = copy_len;\n+        self.anchor = copy_len;\n+        self.scroll_offset = 0;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Clear all content.\n+    pub fn clear(self: *TextInputState) void {\n+        self.len = 0;\n+        self.cursor = 0;\n+        self.anchor = 0;\n+        self.scroll_offset = 0;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Get maximum allowed length.\n+    fn maxLength(self: TextInputState) usize {\n+        if (self.max_len > 0) {\n+            return @min(self.max_len, self.buffer.len);\n+        }\n+        return self.buffer.len;\n+    }\n+\n+    // ========================================\n+    // Cursor Movement\n+    // ========================================\n+\n+    /// Move cursor left by one character.\n+    pub fn cursorLeft(self: *TextInputState) void {\n+        if (self.cursor > 0) {\n+            self.cursor = self.prevCharBoundary(self.cursor);\n+        }\n+        self.anchor = self.cursor;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Move cursor right by one character.\n+    pub fn cursorRight(self: *TextInputState) void {\n+        if (self.cursor < self.len) {\n+            self.cursor = self.nextCharBoundary(self.cursor);\n+        }\n+        self.anchor = self.cursor;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Move cursor to start of line.\n+    pub fn cursorHome(self: *TextInputState) void {\n+        self.cursor = 0;\n+        self.anchor = 0;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Move cursor to end of line.\n+    pub fn cursorEnd(self: *TextInputState) void {\n+        self.cursor = self.len;\n+        self.anchor = self.len;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Move cursor left by one word.\n+    pub fn cursorWordLeft(self: *TextInputState) void {\n+        self.cursor = self.findWordBoundaryLeft(self.cursor);\n+        self.anchor = self.cursor;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Move cursor right by one word.\n+    pub fn cursorWordRight(self: *TextInputState) void {\n+        self.cursor = self.findWordBoundaryRight(self.cursor);\n+        self.anchor = self.cursor;\n+    }\n+\n+    // ========================================\n+    // Selection\n+    // ========================================\n+\n+    /// Check if there is an active selection.\n+    pub fn hasSelection(self: TextInputState) bool {\n+        return self.cursor != self.anchor;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Get the selection range [start, end).\n+    pub fn selectionRange(self: TextInputState) struct { start: usize, end: usize } {\n+        return .{\n+            .start = @min(self.cursor, self.anchor),\n+            .end = @max(self.cursor, self.anchor),\n+        };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Get the selected text.\n+    pub fn selectedText(self: TextInputState) []const u8 {\n+        const range = self.selectionRange();\n+        return self.buffer[range.start..range.end];\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Clear selection (keep cursor position).\n+    pub fn clearSelection(self: *TextInputState) void {\n+        self.anchor = self.cursor;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Select all text.\n+    pub fn selectAll(self: *TextInputState) void {\n+        self.anchor = 0;\n+        self.cursor = self.len;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Extend selection left by one character.\n+    pub fn selectLeft(self: *TextInputState) void {\n+        if (self.cursor > 0) {\n+            self.cursor = self.prevCharBoundary(self.cursor);\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Extend selection right by one character.\n+    pub fn selectRight(self: *TextInputState) void {\n+        if (self.cursor < self.len) {\n+            self.cursor = self.nextCharBoundary(self.cursor);\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Extend selection to start of line.\n+    pub fn selectToStart(self: *TextInputState) void {\n+        self.cursor = 0;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Extend selection to end of line.\n+    pub fn selectToEnd(self: *TextInputState) void {\n+        self.cursor = self.len;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Extend selection left by one word.\n+    pub fn selectWordLeft(self: *TextInputState) void {\n+        self.cursor = self.findWordBoundaryLeft(self.cursor);\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Extend selection right by one word.\n+    pub fn selectWordRight(self: *TextInputState) void {\n+        self.cursor = self.findWordBoundaryRight(self.cursor);\n+    }\n+\n+    // ========================================\n+    // Editing\n+    // ========================================\n+\n+    /// Insert a character at cursor position.\n+    /// Replaces selection if active.\n+    pub fn insertChar(self: *TextInputState, char: u21) void {\n+        var utf8_buf: [4]u8 = undefined;\n+        const utf8_len = std.unicode.utf8Encode(char, &utf8_buf) catch return;\n+        self.insertBytes(utf8_buf[0..utf8_len]);\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Insert text at cursor position.\n+    /// Replaces selection if active.\n+    pub fn insertBytes(self: *TextInputState, bytes: []const u8) void {\n+        // Delete selection first if present\n+        if (self.hasSelection()) {\n+            self.deleteSelection();\n+        }\n+\n+        const max = self.maxLength();\n+        const available = max -| self.len;\n+        const insert_len = @min(bytes.len, available);\n+        if (insert_len == 0) return;\n+\n+        // Make room by shifting content after cursor\n+        const after_cursor = self.len - self.cursor;\n+        if (after_cursor > 0) {\n+            std.mem.copyBackwards(\n+                u8,\n+                self.buffer[self.cursor + insert_len .. self.len + insert_len],\n+                self.buffer[self.cursor..self.len],\n+            );\n+        }\n+\n+        // Insert new content\n+        @memcpy(self.buffer[self.cursor .. self.cursor + insert_len], bytes[0..insert_len]);\n+        self.len += insert_len;\n+        self.cursor += insert_len;\n+        self.anchor = self.cursor;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Delete character before cursor (backspace).\n+    pub fn deleteBackward(self: *TextInputState) void {\n+        if (self.hasSelection()) {\n+            self.deleteSelection();\n+            return;\n+        }\n+\n+        if (self.cursor == 0) return;\n+\n+        const prev = self.prevCharBoundary(self.cursor);\n+        const delete_len = self.cursor - prev;\n+\n+        // Shift content after cursor\n+        const after = self.len - self.cursor;\n+        if (after > 0) {\n+            std.mem.copyForwards(\n+                u8,\n+                self.buffer[prev .. prev + after],\n+                self.buffer[self.cursor..self.len],\n+            );\n+        }\n+\n+        self.len -= delete_len;\n+        self.cursor = prev;\n+        self.anchor = prev;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Delete character at cursor (delete key).\n+    pub fn deleteForward(self: *TextInputState) void {\n+        if (self.hasSelection()) {\n+            self.deleteSelection();\n+            return;\n+        }\n+\n+        if (self.cursor >= self.len) return;\n+\n+        const next = self.nextCharBoundary(self.cursor);\n+        const delete_len = next - self.cursor;\n+\n+        // Shift content after deleted character\n+        const after = self.len - next;\n+        if (after > 0) {\n+            std.mem.copyForwards(\n+                u8,\n+                self.buffer[self.cursor .. self.cursor + after],\n+                self.buffer[next..self.len],\n+            );\n+        }\n+\n+        self.len -= delete_len;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Delete word before cursor.\n+    pub fn deleteWordBackward(self: *TextInputState) void {\n+        if (self.hasSelection()) {\n+            self.deleteSelection();\n+            return;\n+        }\n+\n+        const target = self.findWordBoundaryLeft(self.cursor);\n+        if (target == self.cursor) return;\n+\n+        const delete_len = self.cursor - target;\n+        const after = self.len - self.cursor;\n+        if (after > 0) {\n+            std.mem.copyForwards(\n+                u8,\n+                self.buffer[target .. target + after],\n+                self.buffer[self.cursor..self.len],\n+            );\n+        }\n+\n+        self.len -= delete_len;\n+        self.cursor = target;\n+        self.anchor = target;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Delete word after cursor.\n+    pub fn deleteWordForward(self: *TextInputState) void {\n+        if (self.hasSelection()) {\n+            self.deleteSelection();\n+            return;\n+        }\n+\n+        const target = self.findWordBoundaryRight(self.cursor);\n+        if (target == self.cursor) return;\n+\n+        const delete_len = target - self.cursor;\n+        const after = self.len - target;\n+        if (after > 0) {\n+            std.mem.copyForwards(\n+                u8,\n+                self.buffer[self.cursor .. self.cursor + after],\n+                self.buffer[target..self.len],\n+            );\n+        }\n+\n+        self.len -= delete_len;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Delete the current selection.\n+    fn deleteSelection(self: *TextInputState) void {\n+        if (!self.hasSelection()) return;\n+\n+        const range = self.selectionRange();\n+        const delete_len = range.end - range.start;\n+        const after = self.len - range.end;\n+\n+        if (after > 0) {\n+            std.mem.copyForwards(\n+                u8,\n+                self.buffer[range.start .. range.start + after],\n+                self.buffer[range.end..self.len],\n+            );\n+        }\n+\n+        self.len -= delete_len;\n+        self.cursor = range.start;\n+        self.anchor = range.start;\n+    }\n+\n+    // ========================================\n+    // Clipboard Operations\n+    // ========================================\n+\n+    /// Copy selected text to provided buffer.\n+    /// Returns the copied text slice, or empty if no selection.\n+    pub fn copyTo(self: TextInputState, dest: []u8) []const u8 {\n+        if (!self.hasSelection()) return dest[0..0];\n+\n+        const selected = self.selectedText();\n+        const copy_len = @min(selected.len, dest.len);\n+        @memcpy(dest[0..copy_len], selected[0..copy_len]);\n+        return dest[0..copy_len];\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Cut selected text to provided buffer.\n+    /// Returns the cut text slice, or empty if no selection.\n+    pub fn cutTo(self: *TextInputState, dest: []u8) []const u8 {\n+        const copied = self.copyTo(dest);\n+        if (copied.len > 0) {\n+            self.deleteSelection();\n+        }\n+        return copied;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Paste text from provided slice.\n+    pub fn paste(self: *TextInputState, content: []const u8) void {\n+        self.insertBytes(content);\n+    }\n+\n+    // ========================================\n+    // Input Handling\n+    // ========================================\n+\n+    /// Handle keyboard input.\n+    /// Returns true if the event was handled.\n+    pub fn handleKey(self: *TextInputState, key: Key) bool {\n+        const ctrl = key.modifiers.ctrl;\n+        const shift = key.modifiers.shift;\n+\n+        switch (key.code) {\n+            .char => |c| {\n+                if (ctrl) {\n+                    // Ctrl+key shortcuts\n+                    switch (c) {\n+                        'a' => {\n+                            self.selectAll();\n+                            return true;\n+                        },\n+                        'w' => {\n+                            self.deleteWordBackward();\n+                            return true;\n+                        },\n+                        'u' => {\n+                            self.clear();\n+                            return true;\n+                        },\n+                        else => {},\n+                    }\n+                    return false;\n+                }\n+                // Regular character input\n+                self.insertChar(c);\n+                return true;\n+            },\n+            .left => {\n+                if (ctrl and shift) {\n+                    self.selectWordLeft();\n+                } else if (ctrl) {\n+                    self.cursorWordLeft();\n+                } else if (shift) {\n+                    self.selectLeft();\n+                } else {\n+                    self.cursorLeft();\n+                }\n+                return true;\n+            },\n+            .right => {\n+                if (ctrl and shift) {\n+                    self.selectWordRight();\n+                } else if (ctrl) {\n+                    self.cursorWordRight();\n+                } else if (shift) {\n+                    self.selectRight();\n+                } else {\n+                    self.cursorRight();\n+                }\n+                return true;\n+            },\n+            .home => {\n+                if (shift) {\n+                    self.selectToStart();\n+                } else {\n+                    self.cursorHome();\n+                }\n+                return true;\n+            },\n+            .end => {\n+                if (shift) {\n+                    self.selectToEnd();\n+                } else {\n+                    self.cursorEnd();\n+                }\n+                return true;\n+            },\n+            .backspace => {\n+                if (ctrl) {\n+                    self.deleteWordBackward();\n+                } else {\n+                    self.deleteBackward();\n+                }\n+                return true;\n+            },\n+            .delete => {\n+                if (ctrl) {\n+                    self.deleteWordForward();\n+                } else {\n+                    self.deleteForward();\n+                }\n+                return true;\n+            },\n+            else => {},\n+        }\n+        return false;\n+    }\n+\n+    // ========================================\n+    // UTF-8 Helpers\n+    // ========================================\n+\n+    /// Find the previous character boundary.\n+    fn prevCharBoundary(self: TextInputState, pos: usize) usize {\n+        if (pos == 0) return 0;\n+        var i = pos - 1;\n+        while (i > 0 and !isCharStart(self.buffer[i])) {\n+            i -= 1;\n+        }\n+        return i;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Find the next character boundary.\n+    fn nextCharBoundary(self: TextInputState, pos: usize) usize {\n+        if (pos >= self.len) return self.len;\n+        var i = pos + 1;\n+        while (i < self.len and !isCharStart(self.buffer[i])) {\n+            i += 1;\n+        }\n+        return i;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Check if byte is a UTF-8 character start.\n+    fn isCharStart(byte: u8) bool {\n+        return (byte & 0xC0) != 0x80;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Check if character is a word character.\n+    fn isWordChar(char: u8) bool {\n+        return std.ascii.isAlphanumeric(char) or char == '_';\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Find word boundary to the left.\n+    fn findWordBoundaryLeft(self: TextInputState, pos: usize) usize {\n+        if (pos == 0) return 0;\n+\n+        var i = pos;\n+\n+        // Skip any non-word characters immediately before cursor\n+        while (i > 0 and !isWordChar(self.buffer[i - 1])) {\n+            i -= 1;\n+        }\n+\n+        // Skip word characters\n+        while (i > 0 and isWordChar(self.buffer[i - 1])) {\n+            i -= 1;\n+        }\n+\n+        return i;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Find word boundary to the right.\n+    fn findWordBoundaryRight(self: TextInputState, pos: usize) usize {\n+        if (pos >= self.len) return self.len;\n+\n+        var i = pos;\n+\n+        // Skip word characters at cursor\n+        while (i < self.len and isWordChar(self.buffer[i])) {\n+            i += 1;\n+        }\n+\n+        // Skip any non-word characters\n+        while (i < self.len and !isWordChar(self.buffer[i])) {\n+            i += 1;\n+        }\n+\n+        return i;\n+    }\n+\n+    // ========================================\n+    // Display Helpers\n+    // ========================================\n+\n+    /// Calculate the display width of text up to a byte position.\n+    pub fn displayWidthTo(self: TextInputState, byte_pos: usize) usize {\n+        var width: usize = 0;\n+        var i: usize = 0;\n+        const content = self.buffer[0..@min(byte_pos, self.len)];\n+\n+        while (i < content.len) {\n+            const byte = content[i];\n+            if (byte < 0x80) {\n+                width += 1;\n+                i += 1;\n+            } else {\n+                const char_len = std.unicode.utf8ByteSequenceLength(byte) catch {\n+                    i += 1;\n+                    continue;\n+                };\n+                if (i + char_len <= content.len) {\n+                    const codepoint = std.unicode.utf8Decode(content[i..][0..char_len]) catch {\n+                        i += 1;\n+                        continue;\n+                    };\n+                    // Rough approximation: CJK and emoji are double-width\n+                    if (codepoint >= 0x1100) {\n+                        width += 2;\n+                    } else {\n+                        width += 1;\n+                    }\n+                }\n+                i += char_len;\n+            }\n+        }\n+        return width;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Update scroll offset to keep cursor visible.\n+    pub fn updateScrollOffset(self: *TextInputState, viewport_width: u16) void {\n+        if (viewport_width == 0) return;\n+\n+        const cursor_display_pos = self.displayWidthTo(self.cursor);\n+        const vw: usize = viewport_width;\n+\n+        if (cursor_display_pos < self.scroll_offset) {\n+            self.scroll_offset = cursor_display_pos;\n+        } else if (cursor_display_pos >= self.scroll_offset + vw) {\n+            self.scroll_offset = cursor_display_pos -| (vw -| 1);\n+        }\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+/// TextInput widget for rendering text input fields.\n+pub const TextInput = struct {\n+    /// Text input state.\n+    state: *TextInputState,\n+\n+    /// Default text style.\n+    style: Style = Style.empty,\n+\n+    /// Cursor style (when focused).\n+    cursor_style: Style = Style.init().reverse(),\n+\n+    /// Selection highlight style.\n+    selection_style: Style = Style.init().bg(.blue),\n+\n+    /// Placeholder text when empty.\n+    placeholder: []const u8 = \"\",\n+\n+    /// Placeholder style.\n+    placeholder_style: Style = Style.init().dim(),\n+\n+    /// Whether the input is focused (shows cursor).\n+    focused: bool = true,\n+\n+    /// Render the text input into the buffer.\n+    pub fn render(self: TextInput, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n+        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n+\n+        // Update scroll offset based on viewport\n+        self.state.updateScrollOffset(area.width);\n+\n+        // Fill background\n+        buf.fill(area, Cell.styled(' ', self.style));\n+\n+        const content = self.state.text();\n+\n+        // Show placeholder if empty and not focused\n+        if (content.len == 0 and self.placeholder.len > 0 and !self.focused) {\n+            buf.setString(area.x, area.y, self.placeholder, self.placeholder_style);\n+            return;\n+        }\n+\n+        // Render visible text\n+        const selection = self.state.selectionRange();\n+        const scroll = self.state.scroll_offset;\n+\n+        var x: u16 = area.x;\n+        var byte_idx: usize = 0;\n+        var display_idx: usize = 0;\n+\n+        while (byte_idx < content.len and x < area.right()) {\n+            const byte = content[byte_idx];\n+            const char_len = if (byte < 0x80)\n+                @as(usize, 1)\n+            else\n+                std.unicode.utf8ByteSequenceLength(byte) catch 1;\n+\n+            if (byte_idx + char_len > content.len) break;\n+\n+            const codepoint = if (byte < 0x80)\n+                @as(u21, byte)\n+            else\n+                std.unicode.utf8Decode(content[byte_idx..][0..char_len]) catch byte;\n+\n+            // Rough display width\n+            const char_width: usize = if (codepoint >= 0x1100) 2 else 1;\n+\n+            // Check if this character is visible\n+            if (display_idx + char_width > scroll) {\n+                // Determine style\n+                var char_style = self.style;\n+                const in_selection = self.state.hasSelection() and\n+                    byte_idx >= selection.start and byte_idx < selection.end;\n+\n+                if (in_selection) {\n+                    char_style = self.selection_style;\n+                }\n+\n+                // Draw cursor\n+                if (self.focused and byte_idx == self.state.cursor) {\n+                    char_style = self.cursor_style;\n+                }\n+\n+                buf.set(x, area.y, Cell.styled(codepoint, char_style));\n+                x += @intCast(@min(char_width, area.right() - x));\n+            }\n+\n+            display_idx += char_width;\n+            byte_idx += char_len;\n+        }\n+\n+        // Draw cursor at end if needed\n+        if (self.focused and self.state.cursor >= self.state.len) {\n+            if (x < area.right()) {\n+                buf.set(x, area.y, Cell.styled(' ', self.cursor_style));\n+            }\n+        }\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+// ============================================================\n+// SANITY TESTS - TextInputState basic functionality\n+// ============================================================\n+\n+test
