{"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01GjyDKNKHgfsfHTPczzKvD9","type":"tool_result","content":"     1// Animation helpers for zithril TUI framework\n     2// Provides easing functions, duration tracking, and frame interpolation\n     3// for smooth animations driven by tick events.\n     4//\n     5// Usage:\n     6//   1. Create an Animation with a duration and easing function\n     7//   2. Call update(delta_ms) each tick to advance the animation\n     8//   3. Use progress() or value() to get the current interpolated value\n     9//   4. Check isComplete() to know when to stop\n    10\n    11const std = @import(\"std\");\n    12\n    13/// Easing functions for animation curves.\n    14/// All functions map input [0.0, 1.0] to output [0.0, 1.0].\n    15pub const Easing = enum {\n    16    /// Constant velocity (no acceleration).\n    17    linear,\n    18\n    19    /// Slow start, accelerating.\n    20    ease_in,\n    21\n    22    /// Slow end, decelerating.\n    23    ease_out,\n    24\n    25    /// Slow start and end.\n    26    ease_in_out,\n    27\n    28    /// Quadratic ease in (t^2).\n    29    quad_in,\n    30\n    31    /// Quadratic ease out.\n    32    quad_out,\n    33\n    34    /// Quadratic ease in-out.\n    35    quad_in_out,\n    36\n    37    /// Cubic ease in (t^3).\n    38    cubic_in,\n    39\n    40    /// Cubic ease out.\n    41    cubic_out,\n    42\n    43    /// Cubic ease in-out.\n    44    cubic_in_out,\n    45\n    46    /// Elastic bounce at end.\n    47    elastic_out,\n    48\n    49    /// Overshoot and settle back.\n    50    back_out,\n    51\n    52    /// Multiple bounces at end.\n    53    bounce_out,\n    54\n    55    /// Apply the easing function to a progress value [0.0, 1.0].\n    56    pub fn apply(self: Easing, t: f32) f32 {\n    57        const clamped = @min(1.0, @max(0.0, t));\n    58        return switch (self) {\n    59            .linear => clamped,\n    60            .ease_in => easeInCubic(clamped),\n    61            .ease_out => easeOutCubic(clamped),\n    62            .ease_in_out => easeInOutCubic(clamped),\n    63            .quad_in => clamped * clamped,\n    64            .quad_out => 1.0 - (1.0 - clamped) * (1.0 - clamped),\n    65            .quad_in_out => quadInOut(clamped),\n    66            .cubic_in => easeInCubic(clamped),\n    67            .cubic_out => easeOutCubic(clamped),\n    68            .cubic_in_out => easeInOutCubic(clamped),\n    69            .elastic_out => elasticOut(clamped),\n    70            .back_out => backOut(clamped),\n    71            .bounce_out => bounceOut(clamped),\n    72        };\n    73    }\n    74\n    75    fn easeInCubic(t: f32) f32 {\n    76        return t * t * t;\n    77    }\n    78\n    79    fn easeOutCubic(t: f32) f32 {\n    80        const u = 1.0 - t;\n    81        return 1.0 - u * u * u;\n    82    }\n    83\n    84    fn easeInOutCubic(t: f32) f32 {\n    85        if (t < 0.5) {\n    86            return 4.0 * t * t * t;\n    87        } else {\n    88            const u = -2.0 * t + 2.0;\n    89            return 1.0 - u * u * u / 2.0;\n    90        }\n    91    }\n    92\n    93    fn quadInOut(t: f32) f32 {\n    94        if (t < 0.5) {\n    95            return 2.0 * t * t;\n    96        } else {\n    97            return 1.0 - (-2.0 * t + 2.0) * (-2.0 * t + 2.0) / 2.0;\n    98        }\n    99    }\n   100\n   101    fn elasticOut(t: f32) f32 {\n   102        if (t == 0.0) return 0.0;\n   103        if (t == 1.0) return 1.0;\n   104\n   105        const c4 = (2.0 * std.math.pi) / 3.0;\n   106        return std.math.pow(f32, 2.0, -10.0 * t) * @sin((t * 10.0 - 0.75) * c4) + 1.0;\n   107    }\n   108\n   109    fn backOut(t: f32) f32 {\n   110        const c1: f32 = 1.70158;\n   111        const c3 = c1 + 1.0;\n   112        const u = t - 1.0;\n   113        return 1.0 + c3 * u * u * u + c1 * u * u;\n   114    }\n   115\n   116    fn bounceOut(t: f32) f32 {\n   117        const n1: f32 = 7.5625;\n   118        const d1: f32 = 2.75;\n   119\n   120        if (t < 1.0 / d1) {\n   121            return n1 * t * t;\n   122        } else if (t < 2.0 / d1) {\n   123            const adjusted = t - 1.5 / d1;\n   124            return n1 * adjusted * adjusted + 0.75;\n   125        } else if (t < 2.5 / d1) {\n   126            const adjusted = t - 2.25 / d1;\n   127            return n1 * adjusted * adjusted + 0.9375;\n   128        } else {\n   129            const adjusted = t - 2.625 / d1;\n   130            return n1 * adjusted * adjusted + 0.984375;\n   131        }\n   132    }\n   133};\n   134\n   135/// Animation state tracker.\n   136/// Manages timing and progress for a single animation.\n   137pub const Animation = struct {\n   138    /// Total duration in milliseconds.\n   139    duration_ms: u32,\n   140    /// Elapsed time in milliseconds.\n   141    elapsed_ms: u32 = 0,\n   142    /// Easing function to use.\n   143    easing: Easing = .linear,\n   144    /// Whether to loop the animation.\n   145    looping: bool = false,\n   146    /// Whether the animation is paused.\n   147    paused: bool = false,\n   148    /// Direction for ping-pong animations (true = forward).\n   149    forward: bool = true,\n   150\n   151    /// Create a new animation with the given duration.\n   152    pub fn init(duration_ms: u32) Animation {\n   153        return .{ .duration_ms = duration_ms };\n   154    }\n   155\n   156    /// Create an animation with duration and easing.\n   157    pub fn initWithEasing(duration_ms: u32, easing: Easing) Animation {\n   158        return .{ .duration_ms = duration_ms, .easing = easing };\n   159    }\n   160\n   161    /// Update the animation by the given delta time.\n   162    /// Returns true if the animation is still active.\n   163    pub fn update(self: *Animation, delta_ms: u32) bool {\n   164        if (self.paused) return !self.isComplete();\n   165\n   166        self.elapsed_ms +|= delta_ms;\n   167\n   168        if (self.looping and self.elapsed_ms >= self.duration_ms) {\n   169            self.elapsed_ms = self.elapsed_ms % self.duration_ms;\n   170        }\n   171\n   172        return !self.isComplete();\n   173    }\n   174\n   175    /// Get the raw progress (0.0 to 1.0) without easing.\n   176    pub fn rawProgress(self: Animation) f32 {\n   177        if (self.duration_ms == 0) return 1.0;\n   178        const raw_t = @as(f32, @floatFromInt(self.elapsed_ms)) /\n   179            @as(f32, @floatFromInt(self.duration_ms));\n   180        return @min(1.0, raw_t);\n   181    }\n   182\n   183    /// Get the eased progress (0.0 to 1.0).\n   184    pub fn progress(self: Animation) f32 {\n   185        return self.easing.apply(self.rawProgress());\n   186    }\n   187\n   188    /// Interpolate a value between start and end based on current progress.\n   189    pub fn value(self: Animation, start: f32, end: f32) f32 {\n   190        return lerp(start, end, self.progress());\n   191    }\n   192\n   193    /// Interpolate an integer value between start and end.\n   194    pub fn valueInt(self: Animation, start: i32, end: i32) i32 {\n   195        const t = self.progress();\n   196        const result = @as(f32, @floatFromInt(start)) * (1.0 - t) +\n   197            @as(f32, @floatFromInt(end)) * t;\n   198        return @intFromFloat(@round(result));\n   199    }\n   200\n   201    /// Interpolate a u16 value (common for positions).\n   202    pub fn valueU16(self: Animation, start: u16, end: u16) u16 {\n   203        const t = self.progress();\n   204        const s = @as(f32, @floatFromInt(start));\n   205        const e = @as(f32, @floatFromInt(end));\n   206        const result = s * (1.0 - t) + e * t;\n   207        return @intFromFloat(@max(0.0, @round(result)));\n   208    }\n   209\n   210    /// Check if the animation has completed.\n   211    pub fn isComplete(self: Animation) bool {\n   212        if (self.looping) return false;\n   213        return self.elapsed_ms >= self.duration_ms;\n   214    }\n   215\n   216    /// Reset the animation to the beginning.\n   217    pub fn reset(self: *Animation) void {\n   218        self.elapsed_ms = 0;\n   219        self.forward = true;\n   220    }\n   221\n   222    /// Pause the animation.\n   223    pub fn pause(self: *Animation) void {\n   224        self.paused = true;\n   225    }\n   226\n   227    /// Resume the animation.\n   228    pub fn unpause(self: *Animation) void {\n   229        self.paused = false;\n   230    }\n   231\n   232    /// Toggle pause state.\n   233    pub fn togglePause(self: *Animation) void {\n   234        self.paused = !self.paused;\n   235    }\n   236\n   237    /// Set the animation to loop.\n   238    pub fn setLooping(self: *Animation, looping: bool) Animation {\n   239        self.looping = looping;\n   240        return self.*;\n   241    }\n   242};\n   243\n   244/// Keyframe for multi-step animations.\n   245pub const Keyframe = struct {\n   246    /// Value at this keyframe.\n   247    value: f32,\n   248    /// Time position (0.0 to 1.0).\n   249    time: f32,\n   250    /// Easing to use until next keyframe.\n   251    easing: Easing = .linear,\n   252};\n   253\n   254/// Multi-keyframe animation sequence.\n   255pub fn KeyframeAnimation(comptime max_keyframes: usize) type {\n   256    return struct {\n   257        const Self = @This();\n   258\n   259        keyframes: [max_keyframes]Keyframe = undefined,\n   260        count: usize = 0,\n   261        duration_ms: u32,\n   262        elapsed_ms: u32 = 0,\n   263        looping: bool = false,\n   264\n   265        /// Create a new keyframe animation.\n   266        pub fn init(duration_ms: u32) Self {\n   267            return .{ .duration_ms = duration_ms };\n   268        }\n   269\n   270        /// Add a keyframe at the specified time position.\n   271        pub fn addKeyframe(self: *Self, time: f32, val: f32, ease: Easing) bool {\n   272            if (self.count >= max_keyframes) return false;\n   273            self.keyframes[self.count] = .{\n   274                .time = time,\n   275                .value = val,\n   276                .easing = ease,\n   277            };\n   278            self.count += 1;\n   279            return true;\n   280        }\n   281\n   282        /// Update the animation.\n   283        pub fn update(self: *Self, delta_ms: u32) bool {\n   284            self.elapsed_ms +|= delta_ms;\n   285\n   286            if (self.looping and self.elapsed_ms >= self.duration_ms) {\n   287                self.elapsed_ms = self.elapsed_ms % self.duration_ms;\n   288            }\n   289\n   290            return !self.isComplete();\n   291        }\n   292\n   293        /// Get the current interpolated value.\n   294        pub fn value(self: Self) f32 {\n   295            if (self.count == 0) return 0.0;\n   296            if (self.count == 1) return self.keyframes[0].value;\n   297\n   298            const t = @as(f32, @floatFromInt(self.elapsed_ms)) /\n   299                @as(f32, @floatFromInt(self.duration_ms));\n   300            const clamped_t = @min(1.0, @max(0.0, t));\n   301\n   302            // Find surrounding keyframes\n   303            var prev_idx: usize = 0;\n   304            var next_idx: usize = 0;\n   305            for (0..self.count) |i| {\n   306                if (self.keyframes[i].time <= clamped_t) {\n   307                    prev_idx = i;\n   308                }\n   309                if (self.keyframes[i].time >= clamped_t and next_idx == 0) {\n   310                    next_idx = i;\n   311                    break;\n   312                }\n   313            }\n   314\n   315            if (next_idx == 0) next_idx = self.count - 1;\n   316            if (prev_idx == next_idx) return self.keyframes[prev_idx].value;\n   317\n   318            const prev = self.keyframes[prev_idx];\n   319            const next = self.keyframes[next_idx];\n   320\n   321            // Calculate local progress between keyframes\n   322            const time_range = next.time - prev.time;\n   323            if (time_range == 0) return prev.value;\n   324\n   325            const local_t = (clamped_t - prev.time) / time_range;\n   326            const eased_t = prev.easing.apply(local_t);\n   327\n   328            return lerp(prev.value, next.value, eased_t);\n   329        }\n   330\n   331        /// Check if animation is complete.\n   332        pub fn isComplete(self: Self) bool {\n   333            if (self.looping) return false;\n   334            return self.elapsed_ms >= self.duration_ms;\n   335        }\n   336\n   337        /// Reset to beginning.\n   338        pub fn reset(self: *Self) void {\n   339            self.elapsed_ms = 0;\n   340        }\n   341    };\n   342}\n   343\n   344/// Duration helper for converting time units.\n   345pub const Duration = struct {\n   346    ms: u32,\n   347\n   348    pub fn fromMs(ms: u32) Duration {\n   349        return .{ .ms = ms };\n   350    }\n   351\n   352    pub fn fromSeconds(seconds: f32) Duration {\n   353        return .{ .ms = @intFromFloat(seconds * 1000.0) };\n   354    }\n   355\n   356    pub fn fromFrames(frames: u32, fps: u32) Duration {\n   357        if (fps == 0) return .{ .ms = 0 };\n   358        return .{ .ms = (frames * 1000) / fps };\n   359    }\n   360\n   361    pub fn toSeconds(self: Duration) f32 {\n   362        return @as(f32, @floatFromInt(self.ms)) / 1000.0;\n   363    }\n   364\n   365    pub fn toFrames(self: Duration, fps: u32) u32 {\n   366        if (fps == 0) return 0;\n   367        return (self.ms * fps) / 1000;\n   368    }\n   369};\n   370\n   371/// Frame rate tracker for consistent animation timing.\n   372pub const FrameTimer = struct {\n   373    target_fps: u32 = 60,\n   374    frame_duration_ms: u32 = 16,\n   375    accumulated_ms: u32 = 0,\n   376    frame_count: u64 = 0,\n   377\n   378    /// Create a timer targeting the specified FPS.\n   379    pub fn init(target_fps: u32) FrameTimer {\n   380        const fps = if (target_fps == 0) 60 else target_fps;\n   381        return .{\n   382            .target_fps = fps,\n   383            .frame_duration_ms = 1000 / fps,\n   384        };\n   385    }\n   386\n   387    /// Update with elapsed time, returns number of frames to process.\n   388    pub fn update(self: *FrameTimer, delta_ms: u32) u32 {\n   389        self.accumulated_ms +|= delta_ms;\n   390        const frames = self.accumulated_ms / self.frame_duration_ms;\n   391        self.accumulated_ms = self.accumulated_ms % self.frame_duration_ms;\n   392        self.frame_count +|= frames;\n   393        return @intCast(frames);\n   394    }\n   395\n   396    /// Get milliseconds per frame for this timer.\n   397    pub fn msPerFrame(self: FrameTimer) u32 {\n   398        return self.frame_duration_ms;\n   399    }\n   400};\n   401\n   402/// Linear interpolation between two values.\n   403pub fn lerp(a: f32, b: f32, t: f32) f32 {\n   404    return a + (b - a) * t;\n   405}\n   406\n   407/// Inverse linear interpolation: find t given value between a and b.\n   408pub fn inverseLerp(a: f32, b: f32, value: f32) f32 {\n   409    if (a == b) return 0.0;\n   410    return (value - a) / (b - a);\n   411}\n   412\n   413/// Remap a value from one range to another.\n   414pub fn remap(value: f32, in_min: f32, in_max: f32, out_min: f32, out_max: f32) f32 {\n   415    const t = inverseLerp(in_min, in_max, value);\n   416    return lerp(out_min, out_max, t);\n   417}\n   418\n   419/// Smoothstep interpolation (smooth cubic Hermite).\n   420pub fn smoothstep(edge0: f32, edge1: f32, x: f32) f32 {\n   421    const t = @min(1.0, @max(0.0, (x - edge0) / (edge1 - edge0)));\n   422    return t * t * (3.0 - 2.0 * t);\n   423}\n   424\n   425/// Smoother step (quintic interpolation, zero second derivative at edges).\n   426pub fn smootherstep(edge0: f32, edge1: f32, x: f32) f32 {\n   427    const t = @min(1.0, @max(0.0, (x - edge0) / (edge1 - edge0)));\n   428    return t * t * t * (t * (t * 6.0 - 15.0) + 10.0);\n   429}\n   430\n   431// ============================================================\n   432// SANITY TESTS - Basic animation construction\n   433// ============================================================\n   434\n   435test \"sanity: Animation construction\" {\n   436    const anim = Animation.init(1000);\n   437    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u32, 1000), anim.duration_ms);\n   438    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u32, 0), anim.elapsed_ms);\n   439    try std.testing.expect(!anim.isComplete());\n   440}\n   441\n   442test \"sanity: Animation with easing\" {\n   443    const anim = Animation.initWithEasing(500, .ease_out);\n   444    try std.testing.expectEqual(Easing.ease_out, anim.easing);\n   445}\n   446\n   447test \"sanity: Duration conversion from seconds\" {\n   448    const dur = Duration.fromSeconds(1.5);\n   449    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u32, 1500), dur.ms);\n   450}\n   451\n   452test \"sanity: Duration conversion from frames\" {\n   453    const dur = Create an Animation with a duration and easing function\n//   2. Call update(delta_ms) each tick to advance the animation\n//   3. Use progress() or value() to get the current interpolated value\n//   4. Check isComplete() to know when to stop\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\n\n/// Easing functions for animation curves.\n/// All functions map input [0.0, 1.0] to output [0.0, 1.0].\npub const Easing = enum {\n    /// Constant velocity (no acceleration).\n    linear,\n\n    /// Slow start, accelerating.\n    ease_in,\n\n    /// Slow end, decelerating.\n    ease_out,\n\n    /// Slow start and end.\n    ease_in_out,\n\n    /// Quadratic ease in (t^2).\n    quad_in,\n\n    /// Quadratic ease out.\n    quad_out,\n\n    /// Quadratic ease in-out.\n    quad_in_out,\n\n    /// Cubic ease in (t^3).\n    cubic_in,\n\n    /// Cubic ease out.\n    cubic_out,\n\n    /// Cubic ease in-out.\n    cubic_in_out,\n\n    /// Elastic bounce at end.\n    elastic_out,\n\n    /// Overshoot and settle back.\n    back_out,\n\n    /// Multiple bounces at end.\n    bounce_out,\n\n    /// Apply the easing function to a progress value [0.0, 1.0].\n    pub fn apply(self: Easing, t: f32) f32 {\n        const clamped = @min(1.0, @max(0.0, t));\n        return switch (self) {\n            .linear => clamped,\n            .ease_in => easeInCubic(clamped),\n            .ease_out => easeOutCubic(clamped),\n            .ease_in_out => easeInOutCubic(clamped),\n            .quad_in => clamped * clamped,\n            .quad_out => 1.0 - (1.0 - clamped) * (1.0 - clamped),\n            .quad_in_out => quadInOut(clamped),\n            .cubic_in => easeInCubic(clamped),\n            .cubic_out => easeOutCubic(clamped),\n            .cubic_in_out => easeInOutCubic(clamped),\n            .elastic_out => elasticOut(clamped),\n            .back_out => backOut(clamped),\n            .bounce_out => bounceOut(clamped),\n        };\n    }\n\n    fn easeInCubic(t: f32) f32 {\n        return t * t * t;\n    }\n\n    fn easeOutCubic(t: f32) f32 {\n        const u = 1.0 - t;\n        return 1.0 - u * u * u;\n    }\n\n    fn easeInOutCubic(t: f32) f32 {\n        if (t < 0.5) {\n            return 4.0 * t * t * t;\n        } else {\n            const u = -2.0 * t + 2.0;\n            return 1.0 - u * u * u / 2.0;\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn quadInOut(t: f32) f32 {\n        if (t < 0.5) {\n            return 2.0 * t * t;\n        } else {\n            return 1.0 - (-2.0 * t + 2.0) * (-2.0 * t + 2.0) / 2.0;\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn elasticOut(t: f32) f32 {\n        if (t == 0.0) return 0.0;\n        if (t == 1.0) return 1.0;\n\n        const c4 = (2.0 * std.math.pi) / 3.0;\n        return std.math.pow(f32, 2.0, -10.0 * t) * @sin((t * 10.0 - 0.75) * c4) + 1.0;\n    }\n\n    fn backOut(t: f32) f32 {\n        const c1: f32 = 1.70158;\n        const c3 = c1 + 1.0;\n        const u = t - 1.0;\n        return 1.0 + c3 * u * u * u + c1 * u * u;\n    }\n\n    fn bounceOut(t: f32) f32 {\n        const n1: f32 = 7.5625;\n        const d1: f32 = 2.75;\n\n        if (t < 1.0 / d1) {\n            return n1 * t * t;\n        } else if (t < 2.0 / d1) {\n            const adjusted = t - 1.5 / d1;\n            return n1 * adjusted * adjusted + 0.75;\n        } else if (t < 2.5 / d1) {\n            const adjusted = t - 2.25 / d1;\n            return n1 * adjusted * adjusted + 0.9375;\n        } else {\n            const adjusted = t - 2.625 / d1;\n            return n1 * adjusted * adjusted + 0.984375;\n        }\n    }\n};\n\n/// Animation state tracker.\n/// Manages timing and progress for a single animation.\npub const Animation = struct {\n    /// Total duration in milliseconds.\n    duration_ms: u32,\n    /// Elapsed time in milliseconds.\n    elapsed_ms: u32 = 0,\n    /// Easing function to use.\n    easing: Easing = .linear,\n    /// Whether to loop the animation.\n    looping: bool = false,\n    /// Whether the animation is paused.\n    paused: bool = false,\n    /// Direction for ping-pong animations (true = forward).\n    forward: bool = true,\n\n    /// Create a new animation with the given duration.\n    pub fn init(duration_ms: u32) Animation {\n        return .{ .duration_ms = duration_ms };\n    }\n\n    /// Create an animation with duration and easing.\n    pub fn initWithEasing(duration_ms: u32, easing: Easing) Animation {\n        return .{ .duration_ms = duration_ms, .easing = easing };\n    }\n\n    /// Update the animation by the given delta time.\n    /// Returns true if the animation is still active.\n    pub fn update(self: *Animation, delta_ms: u32) bool {\n        if (self.paused) return !self.isComplete();\n\n        self.elapsed_ms +|= delta_ms;\n\n        if (self.looping and self.elapsed_ms >= self.duration_ms) {\n            self.elapsed_ms = self.elapsed_ms % self.duration_ms;\n        }\n\n        return !self.isComplete();\n    }\n\n    /// Get the raw progress (0.0 to 1.0) without easing.\n    pub fn rawProgress(self: Animation) f32 {\n        if (self.duration_ms == 0) return 1.0;\n        const raw_t = @as(f32, @floatFromInt(self.elapsed_ms)) /\n            @as(f32, @floatFromInt(self.duration_ms));\n        return @min(1.0, raw_t);\n    }\n\n    /// Get the eased progress (0.0 to 1.0).\n    pub fn progress(self: Animation) f32 {\n        return self.easing.apply(self.rawProgress());\n    }\n\n    /// Interpolate a value between start and end based on current progress.\n    pub fn value(self: Animation, start: f32, end: f32) f32 {\n        return lerp(start, end, self.progress());\n    }\n\n    /// Interpolate an integer value between start and end.\n    pub fn valueInt(self: Animation, start: i32, end: i32) i32 {\n        const t = self.progress();\n        const result = @as(f32, @floatFromInt(start)) * (1.0 - t) +\n            @as(f32, @floatFromInt(end)) * t;\n        return @intFromFloat(@round(result));\n    }\n\n    /// Interpolate a u16 value (common for positions).\n    pub fn valueU16(self: Animation, start: u16, end: u16) u16 {\n        const t = self.progress();\n        const s = @as(f32, @floatFromInt(start));\n        const e = @as(f32, @floatFromInt(end));\n        const result = s * (1.0 - t) + e * t;\n        return @intFromFloat(@max(0.0, @round(result)));\n    }\n\n    /// Check if the animation has completed.\n    pub fn isComplete(self: Animation) bool {\n        if (self.looping) return false;\n        return self.elapsed_ms >= self.duration_ms;\n    }\n\n    /// Reset the animation to the beginning.\n    pub fn reset(self: *Animation) void {\n        self.elapsed_ms = 0;\n        self.forward = true;\n    }\n\n    /// Pause the animation.\n    pub fn pause(self: *Animation) void {\n        self.paused = true;\n    }\n\n    /// Resume the animation.\n    pub fn unpause(self: *Animation) void {\n        self.paused = false;\n    }\n\n    /// Toggle pause state.\n    pub fn togglePause(self: *Animation) void {\n        self.paused = !self.paused;\n    }\n\n    /// Set the animation to loop.\n    pub fn setLooping(self: *Animation, looping: bool) Animation {\n        self.looping = looping;\n        return self.*;\n    }\n};\n\n/// Keyframe for multi-step animations.\npub const Keyframe = struct {\n    /// Value at this keyframe.\n    value: f32,\n    /// Time position (0.0 to 1.0).\n    time: f32,\n    /// Easing to use until next keyframe.\n    easing: Easing = .linear,\n};\n\n/// Multi-keyframe animation sequence.\npub fn KeyframeAnimation(comptime max_keyframes: usize) type {\n    return struct {\n        const Self = @This();\n\n        keyframes: [max_keyframes]Keyframe = undefined,\n        count: usize = 0,\n        duration_ms: u32,\n        elapsed_ms: u32 = 0,\n        looping: bool = false,\n\n        /// Create a new keyframe animation.\n        pub fn init(duration_ms: u32) Self {\n            return .{ .duration_ms = duration_ms };\n        }\n\n        /// Add a keyframe at the specified time position.\n        pub fn addKeyframe(self: *Self, time: f32, val: f32, ease: Easing) bool {\n            if (self.count >= max_keyframes) return false;\n            self.keyframes[self.count] = .{\n                .time = time,\n                .value = val,\n                .easing = ease,\n            };\n            self.count += 1;\n            return true;\n        }\n\n        /// Update the animation.\n        pub fn update(self: *Self, delta_ms: u32) bool {\n            self.elapsed_ms +|= delta_ms;\n\n            if (self.looping and self.elapsed_ms >= self.duration_ms) {\n                self.elapsed_ms = self.elapsed_ms % self.duration_ms;\n            }\n\n            return !self.isComplete();\n        }\n\n        /// Get the current interpolated value.\n        pub fn value(self: Self) f32 {\n            if (self.count == 0) return 0.0;\n            if (self.count == 1) return self.keyframes[0].value;\n\n            const t = @as(f32, @floatFromInt(self.elapsed_ms)) /\n                @as(f32, @floatFromInt(self.duration_ms));\n            const clamped_t = @min(1.0, @max(0.0, t));\n\n            // Find surrounding keyframes\n            var prev_idx: usize = 0;\n            var next_idx: usize = 0;\n            for (0..self.count) |i| {\n                if (self.keyframes[i].time <= clamped_t) {\n                    prev_idx = i;\n                }\n                if (self.keyframes[i].time >= clamped_t and next_idx == 0) {\n                    next_idx = i;\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n\n            if (next_idx == 0) next_idx = self.count - 1;\n            if (prev_idx == next_idx) return self.keyframes[prev_idx].value;\n\n            const prev = self.keyframes[prev_idx];\n            const next = self.keyframes[next_idx];\n\n            // Calculate local progress between keyframes\n            const time_range = next.time - prev.time;\n            if (time_range == 0) return prev.value;\n\n            const local_t = (clamped_t - prev.time) / time_range;\n            const eased_t = prev.easing.apply(local_t);\n\n            return lerp(prev.value, next.value, eased_t);\n        }\n\n        /// Check if animation is complete.\n        pub fn isComplete(self: Self) bool {\n            if (self.looping) return false;\n            return self.elapsed_ms >= self.duration_ms;\n        }\n\n        /// Reset to beginning.\n        pub fn reset(self: *Self) void {\n            self.elapsed_ms = 0;\n        }\n    };\n}\n\n/// Duration helper for converting time units.\npub const Duration = struct {\n    ms: u32,\n\n    pub fn fromMs(ms: u32) Duration {\n        return .{ .ms = ms };\n    }\n\n    pub fn fromSeconds(seconds: f32) Duration {\n        return .{ .ms = @intFromFloat(seconds * 1000.0) };\n    }\n\n    pub fn fromFrames(frames: u32, fps: u32) Duration {\n        if (fps == 0) return .{ .ms = 0 };\n        return .{ .ms = (frames * 1000) / fps };\n    }\n\n    pub fn toSeconds(self: Duration) f32 {\n        return @as(f32, @floatFromInt(self.ms)) / 1000.0;\n    }\n\n    pub fn toFrames(self: Duration, fps: u32) u32 {\n        if (fps == 0) return 0;\n        return (self.ms * fps) / 1000;\n    }\n};\n\n/// Frame rate tracker for consistent animation timing.\npub const FrameTimer = struct {\n    target_fps: u32 = 60,\n    frame_duration_ms: u32 = 16,\n    accumulated_ms: u32 = 0,\n    frame_count: u64 = 0,\n\n    /// Create a timer targeting the specified FPS.\n    pub fn init(target_fps: u32) FrameTimer {\n        const fps = if (target_fps == 0) 60 else target_fps;\n        return .{\n            .target_fps = fps,\n            .frame_duration_ms = 1000 / fps,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Update with elapsed time, returns number of frames to process.\n    pub fn update(self: *FrameTimer, delta_ms: u32) u32 {\n        self.accumulated_ms +|= delta_ms;\n        const frames = self.accumulated_ms / self.frame_duration_ms;\n        self.accumulated_ms = self.accumulated_ms % self.frame_duration_ms;\n        self.frame_count +|= frames;\n        return @intCast(frames);\n    }\n\n    /// Get milliseconds per frame for this timer.\n    pub fn msPerFrame(self: FrameTimer) u32 {\n        return self.frame_duration_ms;\n    }\n};\n\n/// Linear interpolation between two values.\npub fn lerp(a: f32, b: f32, t: f32) f32 {\n    return a + (b - a) * t;\n}\n\n/// Inverse linear interpolation: find t given value between a and b.\npub fn inverseLerp(a: f32, b: f32, value: f32) f32 {\n    if (a == b) return 0.0;\n    return (value - a) / (b - a);\n}\n\n/// Remap a value from one range to another.\npub fn remap(value: f32, in_min: f32, in_max: f32, out_min: f32, out_max: f32) f32 {\n    const t = inverseLerp(in_min, in_max, value);\n    return lerp(out_min, out_max, t);\n}\n\n/// Smoothstep interpolation (smooth cubic Hermite).\npub fn smoothstep(edge0: f32, edge1: f32, x: f32) f32 {\n    const t = @min(1.0, @max(0.0, (x - edge0) / (edge1 - edge0)));\n    return t * t * (3.0 - 2.0 * t);\n}\n\n/// Smoother step (quintic interpolation, zero second derivative at edges).\npub fn smootherstep(edge0: f32, edge1: f32, x: f32) f32 {\n    const t = @min(1.0, @max(0.0, (x - edge0) / (edge1 - edge0)));\n    return t * t * t * (t * (t * 6.0 - 15.0) + 10.0);\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// SANITY TESTS - Basic animation construction\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"sanity: Animation construction\" {\n    const anim = Animation.init(1000);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u32, 1000), anim.duration_ms);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u32, 0), anim.elapsed_ms);\n    try std.testing.expect(!anim.isComplete());\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: Animation with easing\" {\n    const anim = Animation.initWithEasing(500, .ease_out);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(Easing.ease_out, anim.easing);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: Duration conversion from seconds\" {\n    const dur = Duration.fromSeconds(1.5);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u32, 1500), dur.ms);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: Duration conversion from frames\" {\n    const dur = Duration.fromFrames(60, 60);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u32, 1000), dur.ms);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: FrameTimer construction\" {\n    const timer = FrameTimer.init(60);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u32, 60), timer.target_fps);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u32, 16), timer.frame_duration_ms);\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// BEHAVIOR TESTS - Easing functions\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"behavior: Easing.linear is identity\" {\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(f32, 0.0), Easing.linear.apply(0.0));\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(f32, 0.5), Easing.linear.apply(0.5));\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(f32, 1.0), Easing.linear.apply(1.0));\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: Easing clamps input to [0, 1]\" {\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(f32, 0.0), Easing.linear.apply(-0.5));\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(f32, 1.0), Easing.linear.apply(1.5));\n}\n\ntest Easing.ease_out ends slow\" {\n    const late = Easing.ease_out.apply(0.8);\n    const linear_late: f32 = 0.8;\n    try std.testing.expect(late > linear_late);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: 0, 0), // Maroon\n   169            RGB.init(0, 128, 0), // Green\n   170            RGB.init(128, 128, 0), // Olive\n   171            RGB.init(0, 0, 128), // Navy\n   172            RGB.init(128, 0, 128), // Purple\n   173            RGB.init(0, 128, 128), // Teal\n   174            RGB.init(192, 192, 192), // Silver\n   175            RGB.init(128, 128, 128), // Gray\n   176            RGB.init(255, 0, 0), // Red\n   177            RGB.init(0, 255, 0), // Lime\n   178            RGB.init(255, 255, 0), // Yellow\n   179            RGB.init(0, 0, 255), // Blue\n   180            RGB.init(255, 0, 255), // Fuchsia\n   181            RGB.init(0, 255, 255), // Aqua\n   182            RGB.init(255, 255, 255), // White\n   183        };\n   184\n   185        for (colors, 0..) |c, i| {\n   186            self.palette[i] = c;\n   187        }\n   188        self.palette_size = 16;\n   189    }\n   190\n   191    /// Add a color to the palette.\n   192    pub fn addColor(self: *SixelEncoder, color: RGB) ?u8 {\n   193        if (self.palette_size >= 255) return null;\n   194        self.palette[self.palette_size] = color;\n   195        self.palette_size += 1;\n   196        return self.palette_size - 1;\n   197    }\n   198\n   199    /// Find the closest color in the palette.\n   200    pub fn findClosestColor(self: SixelEncoder, target: RGB) u8 {\n   201        var best_idx: u8 = 0;\n   202        var best_dist: u32 = std.math.maxInt(u32);\n   203\n   204        for (0..self.palette_size) |i| {\n   205            const c = self.palette[i];\n   206            const dr = @as(i32, target.r) - @as(i32, c.r);\n   207            const dg = @as(i32, target.g) - @as(i32, c.g);\n   208            const db = @as(i32, target.b) - @as(i32, c.b);\n   209            const dist: u32 = @intCast(dr * dr + dg * dg + db * db);\n   210\n   211            if (dist < best_dist) {\n   212                best_dist = dist;\n   213                best_idx = @intCast(i);\n   214            }\n   215        }\n   216\n   217        return best_idx;\n   218    }\n   219\n   220    /// Write the Sixel header escape sequence.\n   221    pub fn writeHeader(self: SixelEncoder, writer: anytype) !void {\n   222        // DCS (Device Control String) for Sixel\n   223        // Format: ESC P <params> q\n   224        // params: P1;P2;P3 where P1=aspect ratio, P2=unused, P3=horizontal grid\n   225        const p3: u8 = if (self.use_private_colors) 0 else 1;\n   226        try writer.print(\"\\x1bP{d};{d};{d}q\", .{ self.aspect_ratio, 0, p3 });\n   227    }\n   228\n   229    /// Write a color definition.\n   230    pub fn writeColorDef(self: SixelEncoder, writer: anytype, idx: u8) !void {\n   231        if (idx >= self.palette_size) return;\n   232        const c = self.palette[idx];\n   233        const pct = c.toSixelPercent();\n   234        // Color definition: #<idx>;2;<r>;<g>;<b>\n   235        // 2 = RGB color space\n   236        try writer.print(\"#{d};2;{d};{d};{d}\", .{ idx, pct.r, pct.g, pct.b });\n   237    }\n   238\n   239    /// Write all color definitions.\n   240    pub fn writeAllColorDefs(self: SixelEncoder, writer: anytype) !void {\n   241        for (0..self.palette_size) |i| {\n   242            try self.writeColorDef(writer, @intCast(i));\n   243        }\n   244    }\n   245\n   246    /// Write the Sixel footer (String Terminator).\n   247    pub fn writeFooter(_: SixelEncoder, writer: anytype) !void {\n   248        try writer.writeAll(\"\\x1b\\\\\");\n   249    }\n   250\n   251    /// Encode a row of sixels (6 vertical pixels).\n   252    /// Returns the sixel character for a 6-pixel column.\n   253    pub fn encodeSixel(bitmap: u6) u8 {\n   254        return @as(u8, bitmap) + 63;\n   255    }\n   256\n   257    /// Get escape sequence for selecting a color.\n   258    pub fn selectColor(_: SixelEncoder, writer: anytype, idx: u8) !void {\n   259        try writer.print(\"#{d}\", .{idx});\n   260    }\n   261\n   262    /// Write a graphics new line (move down 6 pixels).\n   263    pub fn writeNewLine(_: SixelEncoder, writer: anytype) !void {\n   264        try writer.writeByte('-');\n   265    }\n   266\n   267    /// Write a carriage return (move to start of current row).\n   268    pub fn writeCR(_: SixelEncoder, writer: anytype) !void {\n   269        try writer.writeByte('$');\n   270    }\n   271};\n   272\n   273/// Kitty graphics protocol encoder.\n   274/// Supports direct pixel data and image references.\n   275pub const KittyEncoder = struct {\n   276    /// Image format.\n   277    pub const Format = enum(u8) {\n   278        /// 24-bit RGB.\n   279        rgb = 24,\n   280        /// 32-bit RGBA.\n   281        rgba = 32,\n   282        /// PNG data.\n   283        png = 100,\n   284    };\n   285\n   286    /// Transmission type.\n   287    pub const Transmission = enum(u8) {\n   288        /// Direct data in escape sequence.\n   289        direct = 'd',\n   290        /// File path.\n   291        file = 'f',\n   292        /// Temporary file path.\n   293        temp_file = 't',\n   294        /// Shared memory.\n   295        shared_memory = 's',\n   296    };\n   297\n   298    /// Action to perform.\n   299    pub const Action = enum(u8) {\n   300        /// Transmit data.\n   301        transmit = 't',\n   302        /// Transmit and display.\n   303        transmit_display = 'T',\n   304        /// Query terminal.\n   305        query = 'q',\n   306        /// Display previously transmitted.\n   307        display = 'p',\n   308        /// Delete images.\n   309        delete = 'd',\n   310        /// Animate frames.\n   311        animate = 'a',\n   312        /// Compose frames.\n   313        compose = 'c',\n   314    };\n   315\n   316    /// Image ID counter.\n   317    next_id: u32 = 1,\n   318\n   319    pub fn init() KittyEncoder {\n   320        return .{};\n   321    }\n   322\n   323    /// Generate a unique image ID.\n   324    pub fn nextImageId(self: *KittyEncoder) u32 {\n   325        const id = self.next_id;\n   326        self.next_id +|= 1;\n   327        return id;\n   328    }\n   329\n   330    /// Write the start of a Kitty graphics command.\n   331    pub fn writeCommandStart(writer: anytype, action: Action) !void {\n   332        try writer.print(\"\\x1b_Ga={c}\", .{@intFromEnum(action)});\n   333    }\n   334\n   335    /// Write an image transmission command.\n   336    pub fn writeTransmit(\n   337        writer: anytype,\n   338        image_id: u32,\n   339        format: Format,\n   340        width: u32,\n   341        height: u32,\n   342        more_data: bool,\n   343    ) !void {\n   344        try writer.print(\"\\x1b_Ga=t,i={d},f={d},s={d},v={d}\", .{\n   345            image_id,\n   346            @intFromEnum(format),\n   347            width,\n   348            height,\n   349        });\n   350        if (more_data) {\n   351            try writer.writeAll(\",m=1\");\n   352        }\n   353    }\n   354\n   355    /// Write a display command.\n   356    pub fn writeDisplay(\n   357        writer: anytype,\n   358        image_id: u32,\n   359        x: u32,\n   360        y: u32,\n   361        cols: ?u32,\n   362        rows: ?u32,\n   363    ) !void {\n   364        try writer.print(\"\\x1b_Ga=p,i={d},x={d},y={d}\", .{ image_id, x, y });\n   365        if (cols) |c| {\n   366            try writer.print(\",c={d}\", .{c});\n   367        }\n   368        if (rows) |r| {\n   369            try writer.print(\",r={d}\", .{r});\n   370        }\n   371    }\n   372\n   373    /// Write a delete command.\n   374    pub fn writeDelete(writer: anytype, image_id: ?u32) !void {\n   375        if (image_id) |id| {\n   376            try writer.print(\"\\x1b_Ga=d,d=i,i={d}\", .{id});\n   377        } else {\n   378            try writer.writeAll(\"\\x1b_Ga=d,d=a\");\n   379        }\n   380        try writeCommandEnd(writer);\n   381    }\n   382\n   383    /// Write base64-encoded data chunk.\n   384    pub fn writeDataChunk(writer: anytype, data: []const u8, is_last: bool) !void {\n   385        try writer.writeAll(\";\");\n   386        try writeBase64(writer, data);\n   387        if (!is_last) {\n   388            try writer.writeAll(\",m=1\");\n   389        }\n   390        try writeCommandEnd(writer);\n   391    }\n   392\n   393    /// Write command terminator.\n   394    pub fn writeCommandEnd(writer: anytype) !void {\n   395        try writer.writeAll(\"\\x1b\\\\\");\n   396    }\n   397};\n   398\n   399/// iTerm2 inline image protocol encoder.\n   400pub const ITerm2Encoder = struct {\n   401    /// Image options.\n   402    pub const Options = struct {\n   403        /// Width in cells (or auto if null).\n   404        width: ?u32 = null,\n   405        /// Height in cells (or auto if null).\n   406        height: ?u32 = null,\n   407        /// Preserve aspect ratio.\n   408        preserve_aspect: bool = true,\n   409        /// Whether image is inline (vs. download).\n   410        inline_image: bool = true,\n   411        /// Name for the image (optional).\n   412        name: ?[]const u8 = null,\n   413    };\n   414\n   415    pub fn init() ITerm2Encoder {\n   416        return .{};\n   417    }\n   418\n   419    /// Write an inline image command.\n   420    pub fn writeImage(\n   421        writer: anytype,\n   422        data: []const u8,\n   423        options: Options,\n   424    ) !void {\n   425        // OSC 1337 ; File=<args> : <base64 data> BEL\n   426        try writer.writeAll(\"\\x1b]1337;File=\");\n   427\n   428        // Write options\n   429        var first = true;\n   430\n   431        if (options.name) |n| {\n   432            try writeParam(writer, &first, \"name\", n);\n   433        }\n   434\n   435        if (options.width) |w| {\n   436            try writeNumParam(writer, &first, \"width\", w);\n   437        }\n   438\n   439        if (options.height) |h| {\n   440            try writeNumParam(writer, &first, \"height\", h);\n   441        }\n   442\n   443        if (options.preserve_aspect) {\n   444            try writeFlagParam(writer, &first, \"preserveAspectRatio\", true);\n   445        }\n   446\n   447        if (options.inline_image) {\n   448            try writeFlagParam(writer, &first, \"inline\", true);\n   449        }\n   450\n   451        try writer.writeAll(\":\");\n   452\n   453        // Write base64-encoded data\n   454        try writeBase64(writer, data);\n   455\n   456        // Terminate with BEL\n   457        try writer.writeByte(0x07);\n   458    }\n   459\n   460    fn writeParam(writer: anytype, first: *bool, key: []const u8, value: []const u8) !void {\n   461        if (!first.*) try writer.writeByte(';');\n   462        first.* = false;\n   463        try writer.writeAll(key);\n   464        try writer.writeByte('=');\n   465        try writer.writeAll(value);\n   466    }\n   467\n   468    fn writeNumParam(writer: anytype, first: *bool, key: []const u8, value: u32) !void {\n   469        if (!first.*) try writer.writeByte(';');\n   470        first.* = false;\n   471        try writer.writeAll(key);\n   472        try writer.print(\"={d}\", .{value});\n   473    }\n   474\n   475    fn writeFlagParam(writer: anytype, first: *bool, key: []const u8, value: bool) !void {\n   476        if (!first.*) try writer.writeByte(';');\n   477        first.* = false;\n   478        try writer.writeAll(key);\n   479        try writer.print(\"={d}\", .{@as(u8, if (value) 1 else 0)});\n   480    }\n   481};\n   482\n   483/// Base64 encoding table.\n   484const base64_chars = \"ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789+/\";\n   485\n   486/// Write base64-encoded data to writer.\n   487fn writeBase64(writer: anytype, data: []const u8) !void {\n   488    var i: usize = 0;\n   489    while (i + 3 <= data.len) : (i += 3) {\n   490        const b0 = data[i];\n   491        const b1 = data[i + 1];\n   492        const b2 = data[i + 2];\n   493\n   494        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[b0 >> 2]);\n   495        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[((b0 & 0x03) << 4) | (b1 >> 4)]);\n   496        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[((b1 & 0x0F) << 2) | (b2 >> 6)]);\n   497        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[b2 & 0x3F]);\n   498    }\n   499\n   500    const remaining = data.len - i;\n   501    if (remaining == 1) {\n   502        const b0 = data[i];\n   503        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[b0 >> 2]);\n   504        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[(b0 & 0x03) << 4]);\n   505        try writer.writeAll(\"==\");\n   506    } else if (remaining == 2) {\n   507        const b0 = data[i];\n   508        const b1 = data[i + 1];\n   509        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[b0 >> 2]);\n   510        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[((b0 & 0x03) << 4) | (b1 >> 4)]);\n   511        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[(b1 & 0x0F) << 2]);\n   512        try writer.writeByte('=');\n   513    }\n   514}\n   515\n   516/// Cross-platform environment variable getter.\n   517fn getEnv(name: []const u8) ?[]const u8 {\n   518    if (is_windows) {\n   519        return std.process.getEnvVarOwned(std.heap.page_allocator, name) catch null;\n   520    } else {\n   521        return std.posix.getenv(name);\n   522    }\n   523}\n   524\n   525// Detect terminal capabilities with GraphicsCapabilities.detect()\n//   2. Check which protocol is supported\n//   3. Use the appropriate encoder to generate escape sequences\n//   4. Write sequences to terminal output\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst builtin = @import(\"builtin\");\n\nconst is_windows = builtin.os.tag == .windows;\n\n/// Graphics protocol types supported by terminals.\npub const GraphicsProtocol = enum {\n    /// No graphics support.\n    none,\n    /// Sixel graphics (VT340+, xterm -ti vt340).\n    sixel,\n    /// Kitty graphics protocol.\n    kitty,\n    /// iTerm2 inline images.\n    iterm2,\n\n    /// Returns the display name of the protocol.\n    pub fn name(self: GraphicsProtocol) []const u8 {\n        return switch (self) {\n            .none => \"none\",\n            .sixel => \"Sixel\",\n            .kitty => \"Kitty\",\n            .iterm2 => \"iTerm2\",\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Returns the maximum theoretical resolution (protocol limit).\n    pub fn maxResolution(self: GraphicsProtocol) struct { width: u32, height: u32 } {\n        return switch (self) {\n            .none => .{ .width = 0, .height = 0 },\n            .sixel => .{ .width = 4096, .height = 4096 },\n            .kitty => .{ .width = 10000, .height = 10000 },\n            .iterm2 => .{ .width = 10000, .height = 10000 },\n        };\n    }\n};\n\n/// Graphics capabilities detected at runtime.\npub const GraphicsCapabilities = struct {\n    /// Best available protocol for this terminal.\n    protocol: GraphicsProtocol = .none,\n    /// Whether Sixel is supported.\n    sixel: bool = false,\n    /// Whether Kitty graphics protocol is supported.\n    kitty: bool = false,\n    /// Whether iTerm2 inline images are supported.\n    iterm2: bool = false,\n    /// Cell width in pixels (if known).\n    cell_width_px: ?u16 = null,\n    /// Cell height in pixels (if known).\n    cell_height_px: ?u16 = null,\n\n    /// Detect graphics capabilities from environment.\n    pub fn detect() GraphicsCapabilities {\n        var caps = GraphicsCapabilities{};\n\n        // Check for Kitty\n        if (getEnv(\"KITTY_WINDOW_ID\") != null) {\n            caps.kitty = true;\n            caps.protocol = .kitty;\n        }\n\n        // Check for iTerm2\n        if (getEnv(\"ITERM_SESSION_ID\") != null or getEnv(\"ITERM_PROFILE\") != null) {\n            caps.iterm2 = true;\n            if (caps.protocol == .none) caps.protocol = .iterm2;\n        }\n\n        // Check for WezTerm (supports iTerm2 protocol)\n        if (getEnv(\"WEZTERM_PANE\") != null or getEnv(\"WEZTERM_UNIX_SOCKET\") != null) {\n            caps.iterm2 = true;\n            caps.kitty = true;\n            if (caps.protocol == .none) caps.protocol = .kitty;\n        }\n\n        // Check TERM for sixel hints\n        if (getEnv(\"TERM\")) |term| {\n            if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, term, \"sixel\") != null or\n                std.mem.indexOf(u8, term, \"vt340\") != null)\n            {\n                caps.sixel = true;\n                if (caps.protocol == .none) caps.protocol = .sixel;\n            }\n\n            if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"xterm\")) {\n                caps.sixel = true;\n                if (caps.protocol == .none) caps.protocol = .sixel;\n            }\n\n            if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"mlterm\")) {\n                caps.sixel = true;\n                if (caps.protocol == .none) caps.protocol = .sixel;\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Check for explicit sixel support\n        if (getEnv(\"SIXEL_SUPPORT\") != null) {\n            caps.sixel = true;\n            if (caps.protocol == .none) caps.protocol = .sixel;\n        }\n\n        return caps;\n    }\n\n    /// Check if any graphics protocol is available.\n    pub fn hasGraphics(self: GraphicsCapabilities) bool {\n        return self.protocol != .none;\n    }\n\n    /// Get the best available protocol.\n    pub fn bestProtocol(self: GraphicsCapabilities) GraphicsProtocol {\n        return self.protocol;\n    }\n};\n\n/// Sixel graphics encoder.\n/// Converts pixel data to Sixel escape sequences.\npub const SixelEncoder = struct {\n    /// Color palette (up to 256 colors for standard Sixel).\n    palette: [256]RGB = undefined,\n    palette_size: u8 = 0,\n    /// Use private color registers (better color accuracy).\n    use_private_colors: bool = true,\n    /// Aspect ratio hint.\n    aspect_ratio: u8 = 1,\n\n    pub const RGB = struct {\n        r: u8,\n        g: u8,\n        b: u8,\n\n        pub fn init(r: u8, g: u8, b: u8) RGB {\n            return .{ .r = r, .g = g, .b = b };\n        }\n\n        pub fn toSixelPercent(self: RGB) struct { r: u8, g: u8, b: u8 } {\n            return .{\n                .r = @intCast((@as(u16, self.r) * 100) / 255),\n                .g = @intCast((@as(u16, self.g) * 100) / 255),\n                .b = @intCast((@as(u16, self.b) * 100) / 255),\n            };\n        }\n    };\n\n    /// Create a new Sixel encoder with default palette.\n    pub fn init() SixelEncoder {\n        var encoder = SixelEncoder{};\n        encoder.initDefaultPalette();\n        return encoder;\n    }\n\n    /// Initialize with a basic 16-color palette.\n    pub fn initDefaultPalette(self: *SixelEncoder) void {\n        const colors = [_]RGB{\n            RGB.init(0, 0, 0), // Black\n            RGB.init(128, 0, 0), // Maroon\n            RGB.init(0, 128, 0), // Green\n            RGB.init(128, 128, 0), // Olive\n            RGB.init(0, 0, 128), // Navy\n            RGB.init(128, 0, 128), // Purple\n            RGB.init(0, 128, 128), // Teal\n            RGB.init(192, 192, 192), // Silver\n            RGB.init(128, 128, 128), // Gray\n            RGB.init(255, 0, 0), // Red\n            RGB.init(0, 255, 0), // Lime\n            RGB.init(255, 255, 0), // Yellow\n            RGB.init(0, 0, 255), // Blue\n            RGB.init(255, 0, 255), // Fuchsia\n            RGB.init(0, 255, 255), // Aqua\n            RGB.init(255, 255, 255), // White\n        };\n\n        for (colors, 0..) |c, i| {\n            self.palette[i] = c;\n        }\n        self.palette_size = 16;\n    }\n\n    /// Add a color to the palette.\n    pub fn addColor(self: *SixelEncoder, color: RGB) ?u8 {\n        if (self.palette_size >= 255) return null;\n        self.palette[self.palette_size] = color;\n        self.palette_size += 1;\n        return self.palette_size - 1;\n    }\n\n    /// Find the closest color in the palette.\n    pub fn findClosestColor(self: SixelEncoder, target: RGB) u8 {\n        var best_idx: u8 = 0;\n        var best_dist: u32 = std.math.maxInt(u32);\n\n        for (0..self.palette_size) |i| {\n            const c = self.palette[i];\n            const dr = @as(i32, target.r) - @as(i32, c.r);\n            const dg = @as(i32, target.g) - @as(i32, c.g);\n            const db = @as(i32, target.b) - @as(i32, c.b);\n            const dist: u32 = @intCast(dr * dr + dg * dg + db * db);\n\n            if (dist < best_dist) {\n                best_dist = dist;\n                best_idx = @intCast(i);\n            }\n        }\n\n        return best_idx;\n    }\n\n    /// Write the Sixel header escape sequence.\n    pub fn writeHeader(self: SixelEncoder, writer: anytype) !void {\n        // DCS (Device Control String) for Sixel\n        // Format: ESC P <params> q\n        // params: P1;P2;P3 where P1=aspect ratio, P2=unused, P3=horizontal grid\n        const p3: u8 = if (self.use_private_colors) 0 else 1;\n        try writer.print(\"\\x1bP{d};{d};{d}q\", .{ self.aspect_ratio, 0, p3 });\n    }\n\n    /// Write a color definition.\n    pub fn writeColorDef(self: SixelEncoder, writer: anytype, idx: u8) !void {\n        if (idx >= self.palette_size) return;\n        const c = self.palette[idx];\n        const pct = c.toSixelPercent();\n        // Color definition: #<idx>;2;<r>;<g>;<b>\n        // 2 = RGB color space\n        try writer.print(\"#{d};2;{d};{d};{d}\", .{ idx, pct.r, pct.g, pct.b });\n    }\n\n    /// Write all color definitions.\n    pub fn writeAllColorDefs(self: SixelEncoder, writer: anytype) !void {\n        for (0..self.palette_size) |i| {\n            try self.writeColorDef(writer, @intCast(i));\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Write the Sixel footer (String Terminator).\n    pub fn writeFooter(_: SixelEncoder, writer: anytype) !void {\n        try writer.writeAll(\"\\x1b\\\\\");\n    }\n\n    /// Encode a row of sixels (6 vertical pixels).\n    /// Returns the sixel character for a 6-pixel column.\n    pub fn encodeSixel(bitmap: u6) u8 {\n        return @as(u8, bitmap) + 63;\n    }\n\n    /// Get escape sequence for selecting a color.\n    pub fn selectColor(_: SixelEncoder, writer: anytype, idx: u8) !void {\n        try writer.print(\"#{d}\", .{idx});\n    }\n\n    /// Write a graphics new line (move down 6 pixels).\n    pub fn writeNewLine(_: SixelEncoder, writer: anytype) !void {\n        try writer.writeByte('-');\n    }\n\n    /// Write a carriage return (move to start of current row).\n    pub fn writeCR(_: SixelEncoder, writer: anytype) !void {\n        try writer.writeByte('$');\n    }\n};\n\n/// Kitty graphics protocol encoder.\n/// Supports direct pixel data and image references.\npub const KittyEncoder = struct {\n    /// Image format.\n    pub const Format = enum(u8) {\n        /// 24-bit RGB.\n        rgb = 24,\n        /// 32-bit RGBA.\n        rgba = 32,\n        /// PNG data.\n        png = 100,\n    };\n\n    /// Transmission type.\n    pub const Transmission = enum(u8) {\n        /// Direct data in escape sequence.\n        direct = 'd',\n        /// File path.\n        file = 'f',\n        /// Temporary file path.\n        temp_file = 't',\n        /// Shared memory.\n        shared_memory = 's',\n    };\n\n    /// Action to perform.\n    pub const Action = enum(u8) {\n        /// Transmit data.\n        transmit = 't',\n        /// Transmit and display.\n        transmit_display = 'T',\n        /// Query terminal.\n        query = 'q',\n        /// Display previously transmitted.\n        display = 'p',\n        /// Delete images.\n        delete = 'd',\n        /// Animate frames.\n        animate = 'a',\n        /// Compose frames.\n        compose = 'c',\n    };\n\n    /// Image ID counter.\n    next_id: u32 = 1,\n\n    pub fn init() KittyEncoder {\n        return .{};\n    }\n\n    /// Generate a unique image ID.\n    pub fn nextImageId(self: *KittyEncoder) u32 {\n        const id = self.next_id;\n        self.next_id +|= 1;\n        return id;\n    }\n\n    /// Write the start of a Kitty graphics command.\n    pub fn writeCommandStart(writer: anytype, action: Action) !void {\n        try writer.print(\"\\x1b_Ga={c}\", .{@intFromEnum(action)});\n    }\n\n    /// Write an image transmission command.\n    pub fn writeTransmit(\n        writer: anytype,\n        image_id: u32,\n        format: Format,\n        width: u32,\n        height: u32,\n        more_data: bool,\n    ) !void {\n        try writer.print(\"\\x1b_Ga=t,i={d},f={d},s={d},v={d}\", .{\n            image_id,\n            @intFromEnum(format),\n            width,\n            height,\n        });\n        if (more_data) {\n            try writer.writeAll(\",m=1\");\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Write a display command.\n    pub fn writeDisplay(\n        writer: anytype,\n        image_id: u32,\n        x: u32,\n        y: u32,\n        cols: ?u32,\n        rows: ?u32,\n    ) !void {\n        try writer.print(\"\\x1b_Ga=p,i={d},x={d},y={d}\", .{ image_id, x, y });\n        if (cols) |c| {\n            try writer.print(\",c={d}\", .{c});\n        }\n        if (rows) |r| {\n            try writer.print(\",r={d}\", .{r});\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Write a delete command.\n    pub fn writeDelete(writer: anytype, image_id: ?u32) !void {\n        if (image_id) |id| {\n            try writer.print(\"\\x1b_Ga=d,d=i,i={d}\", .{id});\n        } else {\n            try writer.writeAll(\"\\x1b_Ga=d,d=a\");\n        }\n        try writeCommandEnd(writer);\n    }\n\n    /// Write base64-encoded data chunk.\n    pub fn writeDataChunk(writer: anytype, data: []const u8, is_last: bool) !void {\n        try writer.writeAll(\";\");\n        try writeBase64(writer, data);\n        if (!is_last) {\n            try writer.writeAll(\",m=1\");\n        }\n        try writeCommandEnd(writer);\n    }\n\n    /// Write command terminator.\n    pub fn writeCommandEnd(writer: anytype) !void {\n        try writer.writeAll(\"\\x1b\\\\\");\n    }\n};\n\n/// iTerm2 inline image protocol encoder.\npub const ITerm2Encoder = struct {\n    /// Image options.\n    pub const Options = struct {\n        /// Width in cells (or auto if null).\n        width: ?u32 = null,\n        /// Height in cells (or auto if null).\n        height: ?u32 = null,\n        /// Preserve aspect ratio.\n        preserve_aspect: bool = true,\n        /// Whether image is inline (vs. download).\n        inline_image: bool = true,\n        /// Name for the image (optional).\n        name: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    };\n\n    pub fn init() ITerm2Encoder {\n        return .{};\n    }\n\n    /// Write an inline image command.\n    pub fn writeImage(\n        writer: anytype,\n        data: []const u8,\n        options: Options,\n    ) !void {\n        // OSC 1337 ; File=<args> : <base64 data> BEL\n        try writer.writeAll(\"\\x1b]1337;File=\");\n\n        // Write options\n        var first = true;\n\n        if (options.name) |n| {\n            try writeParam(writer, &first, \"name\", n);\n        }\n\n        if (options.width) |w| {\n            try writeNumParam(writer, &first, \"width\", w);\n        }\n\n        if (options.height) |h| {\n            try writeNumParam(writer, &first, \"height\", h);\n        }\n\n        if (options.preserve_aspect) {\n            try writeFlagParam(writer, &first, \"preserveAspectRatio\", true);\n        }\n\n        if (options.inline_image) {\n            try writeFlagParam(writer, &first, \"inline\", true);\n        }\n\n        try writer.writeAll(\":\");\n\n        // Write base64-encoded data\n        try writeBase64(writer, data);\n\n        // Terminate with BEL\n        try writer.writeByte(0x07);\n    }\n\n    fn writeParam(writer: anytype, first: *bool, key: []const u8, value: []const u8) !void {\n        if (!first.*) try writer.writeByte(';');\n        first.* = false;\n        try writer.writeAll(key);\n        try writer.writeByte('=');\n        try writer.writeAll(value);\n    }\n\n    fn writeNumParam(writer: anytype, first: *bool, key: []const u8, value: u32) !void {\n        if (!first.*) try writer.writeByte(';');\n        first.* = false;\n        try writer.writeAll(key);\n        try writer.print(\"={d}\", .{value});\n    }\n\n    fn writeFlagParam(writer: anytype, first: *bool, key: []const u8, value: bool) !void {\n        if (!first.*) try writer.writeByte(';');\n        first.* = false;\n        try writer.writeAll(key);\n        try writer.print(\"={d}\", .{@as(u8, if (value) 1 else 0)});\n    }\n};\n\n/// Base64 encoding table.\nconst base64_chars = \"ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789+/\";\n\n/// Write base64-encoded data to writer.\nfn writeBase64(writer: anytype, data: []const u8) !void {\n    var i: usize = 0;\n    while (i + 3 <= data.len) : (i += 3) {\n        const b0 = data[i];\n        const b1 = data[i + 1];\n        const b2 = data[i + 2];\n\n        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[b0 >> 2]);\n        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[((b0 & 0x03) << 4) | (b1 >> 4)]);\n        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[((b1 & 0x0F) << 2) | (b2 >> 6)]);\n        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[b2 & 0x3F]);\n    }\n\n    const remaining = data.len - i;\n    if (remaining == 1) {\n        const b0 = data[i];\n        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[b0 >> 2]);\n        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[(b0 & 0x03) << 4]);\n        try writer.writeAll(\"==\");\n    } else if (remaining == 2) {\n        const b0 = data[i];\n        const b1 = data[i + 1];\n        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[b0 >> 2]);\n        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[((b0 & 0x03) << 4) | (b1 >> 4)]);\n        try writer.writeByte(base64_chars[(b1 & 0x0F) << 2]);\n        try writer.writeByte('=');\n    }\n}\n\n/// Cross-platform environment variable getter.\nfn getEnv(name: []const u8) ?[]const u8 {\n    if (is_windows) {\n        return std.process.getEnvVarOwned(std.heap.page_allocator, name) catch null;\n    } else {\n        return std.posix.getenv(name);\n    }\n}\n\n//   50\n    51    /// Scroll to a specific offset (clamped to valid range).\n    52    pub fn scrollTo(self: *ScrollState, offset: usize) void {\n    53        self.offset = offset;\n    54        self.clampOffset();\n    55    }\n    56\n    57    /// Scroll by a delta amount (positive = down, negative = up).\n    58    pub fn scrollBy(self: *ScrollState, delta: i32) void {\n    59        if pub fn render(self: ScrollView, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n   248        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n   249\n   250        // Update viewport in scroll state\n   251        self.state.setViewport(area.height);\n   252\n   253        // Fill background\n   254        if (!self.style.isEmpty()) {\n   255            buf.fill(area, Cell.styled(' ', self.style));\n   256        }\n   257\n   258        // Draw scrollbar if needed\n   259        if (self.show_scrollbar and self.state.canScroll()) {\n   260            const sb_area = self.scrollbarArea(area);\n   261 scroll state from items.\n   305    pub fn syncState(self: *ScrollableList) void {\n   306        self.scroll.setTotal(self.items.len);\n   307        if (self.selected) |sel| {\n   308            self.scroll.ensureVisible(sel);\n   309        }\n   310    }\n   311\n   312    /// Move selection up.\n   313    pub fn selectPrevious(self: *ScrollableList) void {\n   314        if (self.items.len == 0) return;\n   315        if (self.selected) |sel| {\n   316            if (sel > 0) {\n   317                self.selected = sel - 1;\n   318                self.scroll.ensureVisible(sel - 1);\n   319            }\n   320        } else {\n   321            self.selected = 0;\n   322            self.scroll.ensureVisible(0);\n   323        }\n   324    }\n   325\n   326    /// Move selection down.\n   327    pub fn selectNext(self: *ScrollableList) void {\n   328        if (self.items.len == 0) return;\n   329        if (self.selected) |sel| {\n   330            if (sel + 1 < self.items.len) {\n   331                self.selected = sel + 1;\n   332                self.scroll.ensureVisible(sel + 1);\n   333            }\n   334        } else {\n   335            self.selected = 0;\n   336            self.scroll.ensureVisible(0);\n   337        }\n   338    }\n   339\n   340    /// Select first item.\n   341    pub fn selectFirst(self: *ScrollableList) void {\n   342        if (self.items.len == 0) return;\n   343        self.selected = 0;\n   344        self.scroll.ensureVisible(0);\n   345    }\n   346\n   347    /// Select last item.\n   348    pub fn selectLast(self: *ScrollableList) void {\n   349        if (self.items.len == 0) return;\n   350        self.selected = self.items.len - 1;\n   351        self.scroll.ensureVisible(self.items.len - 1);\n   352    }\n   353\n   354    /// Handle keyboard input for navigation.\n   355    /// Returns true if the event was handled.\n   356    pub fn handleKey(self: *ScrollableList, key: Key) bool {\n   357        switch (key.code) {\n   358            .up => {\n   359                self.selectPrevious();\n   360                return true;\n   361            },\n   362            .down => {\n   363                self.selectNext();\n   364                return true;\n   365            },\n   366            .home => {\n   367                self.selectFirst();\n   368                return true;\n   369            },\n   370            .end => {\n   371                self.selectLast();\n   372                return true;\n   373            },\n   374            .page_up => {\n   375                if (self.items.len == 0) return true;\n   376                if (self.selected) |sel| {\n   377                    const page = self.scroll.viewport;\n   378                    self.selected = sel -| page;\n   379                    self.scroll.ensureVisible(self.selected.?);\n   380                }\n   381                return true;\n   382            },\n   383            .page_down => {\n   384                if (self.items.len == 0) return true;\n   385                if (self.selected) |sel| {\n   386                    const page = self.scroll.viewport;\n   387                    self.selected = @min(sel + page, self.items.len -| 1);\n   388                    self.scroll.ensureVisible(self.selected.?);\n   389                }\n   390                return true;\n   391            },\n   392            else => {},\n   393        }\n   394        return false;\n   395    }\n   396\n   397    /// Render the scrollable list.\n   398    pub fn render(self: ScrollableList, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n   399        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n   400\n   401        // Calculate content area (minus scrollbar if needed)\n   402        const needs_scrollbar = self.show_scrollbar and self.items.len > area.height;\n   403        const content_width = if (needs_scrollbar) area.width -| 1 else area.width;\n   404        const content_area = Rect.init(area.x, area.y, content_width, area.height);\n   405\n   406        if (content_area.isEmpty()) return;\n   407\n   408        const symbol_len: u16 = @intCast(@min(self.highlight_symbol.len, content_area.width));\n   409        const content_start = content_area.x +| symbol_len;\n   410        const text_width = content_area.width -| symbol_len;\n   411\n   412        // Get visible range\n   413        const range = self.scroll.visibleRange();\n   414\n   415        // Render visible items\n   416        var y = content_area.y;\n   417        var item_index = range.start;\n   418        while (item_index < range.end and y < content_area.bottom()) : ({\n   419            y += 1;\n   420            item_index += 1;\n   421        }) {\n   422            const item = self.items[item_index];\n   423            const is_selected = self.selected != null and self.selected.? == item_index;\n   424\n   425            if (is_selected) {\n   426                // Fill the entire row with highlight style\n   427                const row_rect = Rect.init(content_area.x, y, content_area.width, 1);\n   428                buf.fill(row_rect, Cell.styled(' ', self.highlight_style));\n   429\n   430                // Draw highlight symbol\n   431                if (symbol_len > 0) {\n   432                    buf.setString(content_area.x, y, self.highlight_symbol[0..symbol_len], self.highlight_style);\n   433                }\n   434\n   435                // Draw item text with highlight style\n   436                if (text_width > 0) {\n   437                    buf.setString(content_start, y, item, self.highlight_style);\n   438                }\n   439            } else {\n   440                // Draw item text with normal style\n   441                if (text_width > 0) {\n   442                    buf.setString(content_start, y, item, self.style);\n   443                }\n   444            }\n   445        }\n   446\n   447        // Draw scrollbar if needed\n   448        if (needs_scrollbar) {\n   449            const sb_area = Rect.init(area.x +| content_width, area.y, 1, area.height);\n   450            const scrollbar = Scrollbar{\n   451                .total = self.items.len,\n   452                .position = self.scroll.offset,\n   453                .viewport = area.height,\n   454                .style = self.scrollbar_style,\n   455                .thumb_style = self.scrollbar_thumb_style,\n   456                .orientation = .vertical,\n   457            };\n   458            scrollbar.render(sb_area, buf);\n   459        }\n   460    }\n   461\n   462    /// Get the number of items.\n   463    pub fn len(self: ScrollableList) usize {\n   464        return self.items.len;\n   465    }\n   466\n   467    /// Check if empty.\n   468    pub fn isEmpty(self: ScrollableList) bool {\n   469        return self.items.len == 0;\n   470    }\n   471};\n   472\n
