ScrollView widget for zithril TUI framework\n// Virtual scrolling container with scroll state management and scrollbar integration\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst buffer_mod = @import(\"../buffer.zig\");\nconst geometry = @import(\"../geometry.zig\");\nconst style_mod = @import(\"../style.zig\");\nconst scrollbar_mod = @import(\"scrollbar.zig\");\nconst event_mod = @import(\"../event.zig\");\n\npub const Buffer = buffer_mod.Buffer;\npub const Cell = buffer_mod.Cell;\npub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\npub const Style = style_mod.Style;\npub const Scrollbar = scrollbar_mod.Scrollbar;\npub const Orientation = scrollbar_mod.Orientation;\npub const MouseKind = event_mod.MouseKind;\npub const Mouse = event_mod.Mouse;\npub const KeyCode = event_mod.KeyCode;\npub const Key = event_mod.Key;\n\n/// Scroll state for a scrollable container.\n/// Tracks scroll position and provides helpers for navigation.\npub const ScrollState = struct {\n    /// Current vertical scroll offset (first visible row).\n    offset: usize = 0,\n\n    /// Total number of items/rows in the content.\n    total: usize = 0,\n\n    /// Viewport height (number of visible rows).\n    viewport: u16 = 0,\n\n    /// Create a new scroll state.\n    pub fn init(total: usize) ScrollState {\n        return .{ .total = total };\n    }\n\n    /// Update viewport size and clamp offset if needed.\n    pub fn setViewport(self: *ScrollState, viewport: u16) void {\n        self.viewport = viewport;\n        self.clampOffset();\n    }\n\n    /// Update total content size and clamp offset if needed.\n    pub fn setTotal(self: *ScrollState, total: usize) void {\n        self.total = total;\n        self.clampOffset();\n    }\n\n    /// Scroll to a specific offset (clamped to valid range).\n    pub fn scrollTo(self: *ScrollState, offset: usize) void {\n        self.offset = offset;\n        self.clampOffset();\n    }\n\n    /// Scroll by a delta amount (positive = down, negative = up).\n    pub fn scrollBy(self: *ScrollState, delta: i32) void {\n        if (delta < 0) {\n            const abs_delta: usize = @intCast(-delta);\n            self.offset -|= abs_delta;\n        } else {\n            const pos_delta: usize = @intCast(delta);\n            self.offset +|= pos_delta;\n        }\n        self.clampOffset();\n    }\n\n    /// Scroll up by one line.\n    pub fn scrollUp(self: *ScrollState) void {\n        self.scrollBy(-1);\n    }\n\n    /// Scroll down by one line.\n    pub fn scrollDown(self: *ScrollState) void {\n        self.scrollBy(1);\n    }\n\n    /// Scroll up by one page (viewport height).\n    pub fn pageUp(self: *ScrollState) void {\n        self.scrollBy(-@as(i32, @intCast(self.viewport)));\n    }\n\n    /// Scroll down by one page (viewport height).\n    pub fn pageDown(self: *ScrollState) void {\n        self.scrollBy(@as(i32, @intCast(self.viewport)));\n    }\n\n    /// Scroll to the beginning.\n    pub fn scrollToStart(self: *ScrollState) void {\n        self.offset = 0;\n    }\n\n    /// Scroll to the end.\n    pub fn scrollToEnd(self: *ScrollState) void {\n        self.offset = self.maxOffset();\n    }\n\n    /// Ensure a specific index is visible, scrolling if necessary.\n    pub fn ensureVisible(self: *ScrollState, index: usize) void {\n        if (index < self.offset) {\n            self.offset = index;\n        } else if (index >= self.offset + self.viewport) {\n            self.offset = index -| (self.viewport -| 1);\n        }\n        self.clampOffset();\n    }\n\n    /// Get the maximum valid scroll offset.\n    pub fn maxOffset(self: ScrollState) usize {\n        if (self.total <= self.viewport) return 0;\n        return self.total - self.viewport;\n    }\n\n    /// Check if currently at the top.\n    pub fn atStart(self: ScrollState) bool {\n        return self.offset == 0;\n    }\n\n    /// Check if currently at the bottom.\n    pub fn atEnd(self: ScrollState) bool {\n        return self.offset >= self.maxOffset();\n    }\n\n    /// Check if scrolling is needed (content exceeds viewport).\n    pub fn canScroll(self: ScrollState) bool {\n        return self.total > self.viewport;\n    }\n\n    /// Get the range of visible indices [start, end).\n    pub fn visibleRange(self: ScrollState) struct { start: usize, end: usize } {\n        const start = self.offset;\n        const end = @min(self.offset + self.viewport, self.total);\n        return .{ .start = start, .end = end };\n    }\n\n    /// Clamp offset to valid range.\n    fn clampOffset(self: *ScrollState) void {\n        self.offset = @min(self.offset, self.maxOffset());\n    }\n\n    /// Handle keyboard input for scrolling.\n    /// Returns true if the event was handled.\n    pub fn handleKey(self: *ScrollState, key: Key) bool {\n        switch (key.code) {\n            .up => {\n                self.scrollUp();\n                return true;\n            },\n            .down => {\n                self.scrollDown();\n                return true;\n            },\n            .page_up => {\n                self.pageUp();\n                return true;\n            },\n            .page_down => {\n                self.pageDown();\n                return true;\n            },\n            .home => if (key.modifiers.ctrl) {\n                self.scrollToStart();\n                return true;\n            },\n            .end => if (key.modifiers.ctrl) {\n                self.scrollToEnd();\n                return true;\n            },\n            else => {},\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /// Handle mouse scroll events.\n    /// Returns true if the event was handled.\n    pub fn handleMouse(self: *ScrollState, mouse: Mouse) bool {\n        switch (mouse.kind) {\n            .scroll_up => {\n                self.scrollBy(-3);\n                return true;\n            },\n            .scroll_down => {\n                self.scrollBy(3);\n                return true;\n            },\n            else => {},\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n};\n\n/// ScrollView widget configuration.\n/// Wraps content with virtual scrolling and optional scrollbar.\npub const ScrollView = struct {\n    /// Scroll state (tracks position).\n    state: *ScrollState,\n\n    /// Show scrollbar when content exceeds viewport.\n    show_scrollbar: bool = true,\n\n    /// Scrollbar style.\n    scrollbar_style: Style = Style.empty,\n\n    /// Scrollbar thumb style.\n    scrollbar_thumb_style: Style = Style.init().reverse(),\n\n    /// Background style for the viewport.\n    style: Style = Style.empty,\n\n    /// Scrollbar position (right edge by default).\n    scrollbar_on_left: bool = false,\n\n    /// Get the content area (viewport minus scrollbar if shown).\n    pub fn contentArea(self: ScrollView, area: Rect) Rect {\n        if (!self.show_scrollbar or !self.state.canScroll()) {\n            return area;\n        }\n\n        if (self.scrollbar_on_left) {\n            return Rect.init(\n                area.x +| 1,\n                area.y,\n                area.width -| 1,\n                area.height,\n            );\n        } else {\n            return Rect.init(\n                area.x,\n                area.y,\n                area.width -| 1,\n                area.height,\n            );\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Get the scrollbar area.\n    pub fn scrollbarArea(self: ScrollView, area: Rect) Rect {\n        if (self.scrollbar_on_left) {\n            return Rect.init(area.x, area.y, 1, area.height);\n        } else {\n            return Rect.init(area.x +| (area.width -| 1), area.y, 1, area.height);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Render the scrollbar (if needed).\n    pub fn render(self: ScrollView, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n\n        // Update viewport in scroll state\n        self.state.setViewport(area.height);\n\n        // Fill background\n        if (!self.style.isEmpty()) {\n            buf.fill(area, Cell.styled(' ', self.style));\n        }\n\n        // Draw scrollbar if needed\n        if (self.show_scrollbar and self.state.canScroll()) {\n            const sb_area = self.scrollbarArea(area);\n            const scrollbar = Scrollbar{\n                .total = self.state.total,\n                .position = self.state.offset,\n                .viewport = self.state.viewport,\n                .style = self.scrollbar_style,\n                .thumb_style = self.scrollbar_thumb_style,\n                .orientation = .vertical,\n            };\n            scrollbar.render(sb_area, buf);\n        }\n    }\n};\n\n/// ScrollableList combines List behavior with virtual scrolling.\n/// Renders only visible items and integrates with ScrollState.\npub const ScrollableList = struct {\n    /// Items to display.\n    items: []const []const u8,\n\n    /// Scroll state.\n    scroll: *ScrollState,\n\n    /// Currently selected item index (null for no selection).\n    selected: ?usize = null,\n\n    /// Default style for non-selected items.\n    style: Style = Style.empty,\n\n    /// Style for the selected item.\n    highlight_style: Style = Style.init().bg(.blue),\n\n    /// Prefix shown before the selected item.\n    highlight_symbol: []const u8 = \"> \",\n\n    /// Show scrollbar when content exceeds viewport.\n    show_scrollbar: bool = true,\n\n    /// Scrollbar style.\n    scrollbar_style: Style = Style.empty,\n\n    /// Scrollbar thumb style.\n    scrollbar_thumb_style: Style = Style.init().reverse(),\n\n    /// Update scroll state from items.\n    pub fn syncState(self: *ScrollableList) void {\n        self.scroll.setTotal(self.items.len);\n        if (self.selected) |sel| {\n            self.scroll.ensureVisible(sel);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Move selection up.\n    pub fn selectPrevious(self: *ScrollableList) void {\n        if (self.items.len == 0) return;\n        if (self.selected) |sel| {\n            if (sel > 0) {\n                self.selected = sel - 1;\n                self.scroll.ensureVisible(sel - 1);\n            }\n        } else {\n            self.selected = 0;\n            self.scroll.ensureVisible(0);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Move selection down.\n    pub fn selectNext(self: *ScrollableList) void {\n        if (self.items.len == 0) return;\n        if (self.selected) |sel| {\n            if (sel + 1 < self.items.len) {\n                self.selected = sel + 1;\n                self.scroll.ensureVisible(sel + 1);\n            }\n        } else {\n            self.selected = 0;\n            self.scroll.ensureVisible(0);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Select first item.\n    pub fn selectFirst(self: *ScrollableList) void {\n        if (self.items.len == 0) return;\n        self.selected = 0;\n        self.scroll.ensureVisible(0);\n    }\n\n    /// Select last item.\n    pub fn selectLast(self: *ScrollableList) void {\n        if (self.items.len == 0) return;\n        self.selected = self.items.len - 1;\n        self.scroll.ensureVisible(self.items.len - 1);\n    }\n\n    /// Handle keyboard input for navigation.\n    /// Returns true if the event was handled.\n    pub fn handleKey(self: *ScrollableList, key: Key) bool {\n        switch (key.code) {\n            .up => {\n                self.selectPrevious();\n                return true;\n            },\n            .down => {\n                self.selectNext();\n                return true;\n            },\n            .home => {\n                self.selectFirst();\n                return true;\n            },\n            .end => {\n                self.selectLast();\n                return true;\n            },\n            .page_up => {\n                if (self.items.len == 0) return true;\n                if (self.selected) |sel| {\n                    const page = self.scroll.viewport;\n                    self.selected = sel -| page;\n                    self.scroll.ensureVisible(self.selected.?);\n                }\n                return true;\n            },\n            .page_down => {\n                if (self.items.len == 0) return true;\n                if (self.selected) |sel| {\n                    const page = self.scroll.viewport;\n                    self.selected = @min(sel + page, self.items.len -| 1);\n                    self.scroll.ensureVisible(self.selected.?);\n                }\n                return true;\n            },\n            else => {},\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /// Render the scrollable list.\n    pub fn render(self: ScrollableList, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n\n        // Calculate content area (minus scrollbar if needed)\n        const needs_scrollbar = self.show_scrollbar and self.items.len > area.height;\n        const content_width = if (needs_scrollbar) area.width -| 1 else area.width;\n        const content_area = Rect.init(area.x, area.y, content_width, area.height);\n\n        if (content_area.isEmpty()) return;\n\n        const symbol_len: u16 = @intCast(@min(self.highlight_symbol.len, content_area.width));\n        const content_start = content_area.x +| symbol_len;\n        const text_width = content_area.width -| symbol_len;\n\n        // Get visible range\n        const range = self.scroll.visibleRange();\n\n        // Render visible items\n        var y = content_area.y;\n        var item_index = range.start;\n        while (item_index < range.end and y < content_area.bottom()) : ({\n            y += 1;\n            item_index += 1;\n        }) {\n            const item = self.items[item_index];\n            const is_selected = self.selected != null and self.selected.? == item_index;\n\n            if (is_selected) {\n                // Fill the entire row with highlight style\n                const row_rect = Rect.init(content_area.x, y, content_area.width, 1);\n                buf.fill(row_rect, Cell.styled(' ', self.highlight_style));\n\n                // Draw highlight symbol\n                if (symbol_len > 0) {\n                    buf.setString(content_area.x, y, self.highlight_symbol[0..symbol_len], self.highlight_style);\n                }\n\n                // Draw item text with highlight style\n                if (text_width > 0) {\n                    buf.setString(content_start, y, item, self.highlight_style);\n                }\n            } else {\n                // Draw item text with normal style\n                if (text_width > 0) {\n                    buf.setString(content_start, y, item, self.style);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Draw scrollbar if needed\n        if (needs_scrollbar) {\n            const sb_area = Rect.init(area.x +| content_width, area.y, 1, area.height);\n            const scrollbar = Scrollbar{\n                .total = self.items.len,\n                .position = self.scroll.offset,\n                .viewport = area.height,\n                .style = self.scrollbar_style,\n                .thumb_style = self.scrollbar_thumb_style,\n                .orientation = .vertical,\n            };\n            scrollbar.render(sb_area, buf);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Get the number of items.\n    pub fn len(self: ScrollableList) usize {\n        return self.items.len;\n    }\n\n    /// Check if empty.\n    pub fn isEmpty(self: ScrollableList) bool {\n        return self.items.len == 0;\n    }\n};\n\n// ============================================================\n// SANITY TESTS - ScrollState basic functionality\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"sanity: ScrollState default values\" {\n    const state = ScrollState{};\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), state.offset);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), state.total);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 0), state.viewport);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: ScrollState.init\" {\n    const state = ScrollState.init(100);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), state.offset);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 100), state.total);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: ScrollState.setViewport\" {\n    var state = ScrollState.init(100);\n    state.setViewport(20);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 20), state.viewport);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: ScrollState.maxOffset\" {\n    var state = ScrollState.init(100);\n    state.setViewport(20);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 80), state.maxOffset());\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: ScrollState.canScroll\" {\n    var small = ScrollState.init(10);\n    small.setViewport(20);\n    try std.testing.expect(!small.canScroll());\n\n    var large = ScrollState.init(100);\n    large.setViewport(20);\n    try std.testing.expect(large.canScroll());\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// BEHAVIOR TESTS - ScrollState navigation\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"behavior: ScrollState.scrollTo\" {\n    var state = ScrollState.init(100);\n    state.setViewport(20);\n\n    state.scrollTo(50);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 50), state.offset);\n\n    state.scrollTo(90);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 80), state.offset);\n\n    state.scrollTo(0);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), state.offset);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: ScrollState.scrollBy\" {\n    var state = ScrollState.init(100);\n    state.setViewport(20);\n\n    state.scrollBy(10);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 10), state.offset);\n\n    state.scrollBy(-5);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 5), state.offset);\n\n    state.scrollBy(-100);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), state.offset);\n\n    state.scrollBy(200);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 80), state.offset);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: ScrollState.pageUp and pageDown\" {\n    var state = ScrollState.init(100);\n    state.setViewport(20);\n\n    state.scrollTo(50);\n    state.pageUp();\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 30), state.offset);\n\n    state.pageDown();\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 50), state.offset);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: ScrollState.scrollToStart and scrollToEnd\" {\n    var state = ScrollState.init(100);\n    state.setViewport(20);\n\n    state.scrollTo(50);\n    state.scrollToStart();\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), state.offset);\n    try std.testing.expect(state.atStart());\n\n    state.scrollToEnd();\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 80), state.offset);\n    try std.testing.expect(state.atEnd());\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: ScrollState.ensureVisible\" {\n    var state = ScrollState.init(100);\n    state.setViewport(20);\n    state.scrollTo(50);\n\n    // Item already visible\n    state.ensureVisible(55);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 50), state.offset);\n\n    // Item above viewport\n    state.ensureVisible(40);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 40), state.offset);\n\n    // Item below viewport\n    state.ensureVisible(80);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 61), state.offset);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: ScrollState.visibleRange\" {\n    var state = ScrollState.init(100);\n    state.setViewport(20);\n    state.scrollTo(50);\n\n    const range = state.visibleRange();\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 50), range.start);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 70), range.end);\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// BEHAVIOR TESTS - ScrollState input handling\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"behavior: ScrollState.handleKey up/down\" {\n    var state = ScrollState.init(100);\n    state.setViewport(20);\n    state.scrollTo(50);\n\n    const handled_up = state.handleKey(.{ .code = .up });\n    try std.testing.expect(handled_up);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 49), state.offset);\n\n    const handled_down = state.handleKey(.{ .code = .down });\n    try std.testing.expect(handled_down);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 50), state.offset);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: ScrollState.handleKey page up/down\" {\n    var state = ScrollState.init(100);\n    state.setViewport(20);\n    state.scrollTo(50);\n\n    const handled_pgup = state.handleKey(.{ .code = .page_up });\n    try std.testing.expect(handled_pgup);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 30), state.offset);\n\n    const handled_pgdn = state.handleKey(.{ .code = .page_down });\n    try std.testing.expect(handled_pgdn);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 50), state.offset);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: ScrollState.handleMouse scroll\" {\n    var state = ScrollState.init(100);\n    state.setViewport(20);\n    state.scrollTo(50);\n\n    const handled_up = state.handleMouse(.{ .x = 0, .y = 0, .kind = .scroll_up });\n    try std.testing.expect(handled_up);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 47), state.offset);\n\n    const handled_down = state.handleMouse(.{ .x = 0, .y = 0, .kind = .scroll_down });\n    try std.testing.expect(handled_down);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 50), state.offset);\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// SANITY TESTS - ScrollView\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"sanity: ScrollView contentArea\" {\n    var state = ScrollState.init(100);\n    state.setViewport(20);\n\n    const sv = ScrollView{ .state = &state };\n    const area = Rect.init(0, 0, 40, 20);\n\n    const content = sv.contentArea(area);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 0), content.x);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 39), content.width);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: ScrollView scrollbarArea\" {\n    var state = ScrollState.init(100);\n    state.setViewport(20);\n\n    const sv = ScrollView{ .state = &state };\n    const area = Rect.init(0, 0, 40, 20);\n\n    const sb_area = sv.scrollbarArea(area);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 39), sb_area.x);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 1), sb_area.width);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: ScrollView no scrollbar when not needed\" {\n    var state = ScrollState.init(10);\n    state.setViewport(20);\n\n    const sv = ScrollView{ .state = &state };\n    const area = Rect.init(0, 0, 40, 20);\n\n    const content = sv.contentArea(area);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 40), content.width);\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// SANITY TESTS - ScrollableList\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"sanity: ScrollableList default values\" {\n    var state = ScrollState{};\n    const items = [_][]const u8{ \"a\", \"b\", \"c\" };\n    const list = ScrollableList{\n        .items = &items,\n        .scroll = &state,\n    };\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 3), list.len());\n    try std.testing.expect(!list.isEmpty());\n    try std.testing.expect(list.selected == null);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: ScrollableList.syncState\" {\n    var state = ScrollState{};\n    const items = [_][]const u8{ \"a\", \"b\", \"c\", \"d\", \"e\" };\n    var list = ScrollableList{\n        .items = &items,\n        .scroll = &state,\n    };\n    state.setViewport(3);\n\n    list.syncState();\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 5), state.total);\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// BEHAVIOR TESTS - ScrollableList navigation\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"behavior: ScrollableList.selectPrevious and selectNext\" {\n    var state = ScrollState{};\n    state.setViewport(3);\n    const items = [_][]const u8{ \"a\", \"b\", \"c\", \"d\", \"e\" };\n    var list = ScrollableList{\n        .items = &items,\n        .scroll = &state,\n        .selected = 2,\n    };\n    list.syncState();\n\n    list.selectNext();\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(?usize, 3), list.selected);\n\n    list.selectPrevious();\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(?usize, 2), list.selected);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: ScrollableList.selectFirst and selectLast\" {\n    var state = ScrollState{};\n    state.setViewport(3);\n    const items = [_][]const u8{ \"a\", \"b\", \"c\", \"d\", \"e\" };\n    var list = ScrollableList{\n        .items = &items,\n        .scroll = &state,\n        .selected = 2,\n    };\n    list.syncState();\n\n    list.selectFirst();\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(?usize, 0), list.selected);\n\n    list.selectLast();\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(?usize, 4), list.selected);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: ScrollableList selection scrolls into view\" {\n    var state = ScrollState{};\n    state.setViewport(3);\n    const items = [_][]const u8{ \"a\", \"b\", \"c\", \"d\", \"e\", \"f\", \"g\", \"h\" };\n    var list = ScrollableList{\n        .items = &items,\n        .scroll = &state,\n        .selected = 0,\n    };\n    list.syncState();\n\n    // Select last - should scroll\n    list.selectLast();\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(?usize, 7), list.selected);\n    try std.testing.expect(state.offset > 0);\n\n    // Select first - should scroll back\n    list.selectFirst();\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), state.offset);\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// BEHAVIOR TESTS - ScrollableList rendering\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"behavior: ScrollableList renders visible items\" {\n    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 3);\n    defer buf.deinit();\n\n    var state = ScrollState{};\n    state.setViewport(3);\n    const items = [_][]const u8{ \"Alpha\", \"Beta\", \"Gamma\", \"Delta\", \"Epsilon\" };\n    var list = ScrollableList{\n        .items = &items,\n        .scroll = &state,\n        .show_scrollbar = false,\n    };\n    list.syncState();\n\n    list.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 20, 3), &buf);\n\n    // First 3 items should be visible (with highlight symbol offset)\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'A'), buf.get(2, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'B'), buf.get(2, 1).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'G'), buf.get(2, 2).char);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: ScrollableList renders scrolled items\" {\n    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 3);\n    defer buf.deinit();\n\n    var state = ScrollState{};\n    state.setViewport(3);\n    const items = [_][]const u8{ \"Alpha\", \"Beta\", \"Gamma\", \"Delta\", \"Epsilon\" };\n    var list = ScrollableList{\n        .items = &items,\n        .scroll = &state,\n        .show_scrollbar = false,\n    };\n    list.syncState();\n    state.scrollTo(2);\n\n    list.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 20, 3), &buf);\n\n    // Items 2-4 should be visible\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'G'), buf.get(2, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'D'), buf.get(2, 1).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'E'), buf.get(2, 2).char);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: ScrollableList renders with scrollbar\" {\n    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 3);\n    defer buf.deinit();\n\n    var state = ScrollState{};\n    state.setViewport(3);\n    const items = [_][]const u8{ \"Alpha\", \"Beta\", \"Gamma\", \"Delta\", \"Epsilon\" };\n    var list = ScrollableList{\n        .items = &items,\n        .scroll = &state,\n        .show_scrollbar = true,\n        .scrollbar_thumb_style = Style.init().reverse(),\n    };\n    list.syncState();\n\n    list.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 20, 3), &buf);\n\n    // Scrollbar should be in last column\n    const sb_cell = buf.get(19, 0);\n    try Helpers\n   488    // ========================================\n   489\n   490    /// Find the previous character boundary.\n   491    fn prevCharBoundary(self: TextInputState, pos: usize) usize {\n   492        if (pos == 0) return 0;\n   493        var i = pos - 1;\n   494        while (i > 0 and !isCharStart(self.buffer[i])) {\n   495            i -= 1;\n   496        }\n   497        return i;\n   498    }\n   499\n   500    /// Find the next character boundary.\n   501    fn nextCharBoundary(self: TextInputState, pos: usize) usize {\n   502        if (pos >= self.len) return self.len;\n   503        var i = pos + 1;\n   504        while (i < self.len and !isCharStart(self.buffer[i])) {\n   505            i += 1;\n   506        }\n   507        return i;\n   508    }\n   509\n   510    /// Check if byte is a UTF-8 character start.\n   511    fn isCharStart(byte: u8) bool {\n   512        return (byte & 0xC0) != 0x80;\n   513    }\n   514\n   515    /// Check if character is a word character.\n   516    fn isWordChar(char: u8) bool {\n   517        return std.ascii.isAlphanumeric(char) or char == '_';\n   518    }\n   519\n   520    /// Find word boundary to the left.\n   521    fn findWordBoundaryLeft(self: TextInputState, pos: usize) usize {\n   522        if (pos == 0) return 0;\n   523\n   524        var i = pos;\n   525\n   526        // Skip any non-word characters immediately before cursor\n   527        while (i > 0 and !isWordChar(self.buffer[i - 1])) {\n   528            i -= 1;\n   529        }\n   530\n   531        // Skip word characters\n   532        while (i > 0 and isWordChar(self.buffer[i - 1])) {\n   533            i -= 1;\n   534        }\n   535\n   536        return i;\n   537    }\n   538\n   539    /// Find word boundary to the right.\n   540    fn findWordBoundaryRight(self: TextInputState, pos: usize) usize {\n   541        if (pos >= self.len) return self.len;\n   542\n   543        var i = pos;\n   544\n   545        // Skip word characters at cursor\n   546        while (i < self.len and isWordChar(self.buffer[i])) {\n   547            i += 1;\n   548        }\n   549\n   550        // Skip any non-word characters\n   551        while (i < self.len and !isWordChar(self.buffer[i])) {\n   552            i += 1;\n   553        }\n   554\n   555        return i;\n   556    }\n   557\n   558    // ========================================\n   559    // Display Helpers\n   560    // ========================================\n   561\n   562    /// Calculate the display width of text up to a byte position.\n   563    pub fn displayWidthTo(self: TextInputState, byte_pos: usize) usize {\n   564        var width: usize = 0;\n   565        var i: usize = 0;\n   566        const content = self.buffer[0..@min(byte_pos, self.len)];\n   567\n   568        while (i < content.len) {\n   569            const byte = content[i];\n   570            if (byte < 0x80) {\n   571                width += 1;\n   572                i += 1;\n   573            } else {\n   574                const char_len = std.unicode.utf8ByteSequenceLength(byte) catch {\n   575                    i += 1;\n   576                    continue;\n   577                };\n   578                if (i + char_len <= content.len) {\n   579                    const codepoint = std.unicode.utf8Decode(content[i..][0..char_len]) catch {\n   580                        i += 1;\n   581                        continue;\n   582                    };\n   583                    // Rough approximation: CJK and emoji are double-width\n   584                    if (codepoint >= 0x1100) {\n   585                        width += 2;\n   586                    } else {\n   587                        width += 1;\n   588                    }\n   589                }\n   590                i += char_len;\n   591            }\n   592        }\n   593        return width;\n   594    }\n   595\n   596    /// Update scroll offset to keep cursor visible.\n   597    pub fn updateScrollOffset(self: *TextInputState, viewport_width: u16) void {\n   598        if (viewport_width == 0) return;\n   599\n   600        const cursor_display_pos = self.displayWidthTo(self.cursor);\n   601        const vw: usize = viewport_width;\n   602\n   603        if (cursor_display_pos < self.scroll_offset) {\n   604            self.scroll_offset = cursor_display_pos;\n   605        } else if (cursor_display_pos >= self.scroll_offset + vw) {\n   606            self.scroll_offset = cursor_display_pos -| (vw -| 1);\n   607        }\n   608    }\n   609};\n   610\n   611/// TextInput widget for rendering text input fields.\n   612pub const TextInput = struct {\n   613    /// Text input state.\n   614    state: *TextInputState,\n   615\n   616    /// Default text style.\n   617    style: Style = Style.empty,\n   618\n   619    /// Cursor style (when focused).\n   620    cursor_style: Style = Style.init().reverse(),\n   621\n   622    /// Selection highlight style.\n   623    selection_style: Style = Style.init().bg(.blue),\n   624\n   625    /// Placeholder text when empty.\n   626    placeholder: []const u8 = \"\",\n   627\n   628    /// Placeholder style.\n   629    placeholder_style: Style = Style.init().dim(),\n   630\n   631    /// Whether the input is focused (shows cursor).\n   632    focused: bool = true,\n   633\n   634    /// Render the text input into the buffer.\n   635    pub fn render(self: TextInput, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n   636        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n   637\n   638        // Update scroll offset based on viewport\n   639        self.state.updateScrollOffset(area.width);\n   640\n   641        // Fill background\n   642        buf.fill(area, Cell.styled(' ', self.style));\n   643\n   644        const content = self.state.text();\n   645\n   646        // Show placeholder if empty and not focused\n   647        if (content.len == 0 and self.placeholder.len > 0 and !self.focused) {\n   648            buf.setString(area.x, area.y, self.placeholder, self.placeholder_style);\n   649            return;\n   650        }\n   651\n   652        // Render visible text\n   653        const selection = self.state.selectionRange();\n   654        const scroll = self.state.scroll_offset;\n   655\n   656        var x: u16 = area.x;\n   657        var byte_idx: usize = 0;\n   658        var display_idx: usize = 0;\n   659\n   660        while (byte_idx < content.len and x < area.right()) {\n   661            const byte = content[byte_idx];\n   662            const char_len = if (byte < 0x80)\n   663                @as(usize, 1)\n   664            else\n   665                std.unicode.utf8ByteSequenceLength(byte) catch 1;\n   666\n   667            if (byte_idx + char_len > content.len) break;\n   668\n   669            const codepoint = if (byte < 0x80)\n   670                @as(u21, byte)\n   671            else\n   672                std.unicode.utf8Decode(content[byte_idx..][0..char_len]) catch byte;\n   673\n   674            // Rough display width\n   675            const char_width: usize = if (codepoint >= 0x1100) 2 else 1;\n   676\n   677            // Check if this character is visible\n   678            if (display_idx + char_width > scroll) {\n   679                // Determine style\n   680                var char_style = self.style;\n   681                const in_selection = self.state.hasSelection() and\n   682                    byte_idx >= selection.start and byte_idx < selection.end;\n   683\n   684                if (in_selection) {\n   685                    char_style = self.selection_style;\n   686                }\n   687\n   688                // Draw cursor\n   689                if (self.focused and byte_idx == self.state.cursor) {\n   690                    char_style = self.cursor_style;\n   691                }\n   692\n   693                buf.set(x, area.y, Cell.styled(codepoint, char_style));\n   694                x += @intCast(@min(char_width, area.right() - x));\n   695            }\n   696\n   697            display_idx += char_width;\n   698            byte_idx += char_len;\n   699        }\n   700\n   701        // Draw cursor at end if needed\n   702        if (self.focused and self.state.cursor >= self.state.len) {\n   703            if (x < area.right()) {\n   704                buf.set(x, area.y, Cell.styled(' ', self.cursor_style));\n   705            }\n   706        }\n   707    }\n If different from cursor, text is selected.\n    /// Selection range is [min(anchor, cursor), max(anchor, cursor)).\n    anchor: usize = 0,\n\n    /// Horizontal scroll offset (for text wider than viewport).\n    scroll_offset: usize = 0,\n\n    /// Maximum allowed content length (0 = use buffer size).\n    max_len: usize = 0,\n\n    /// Create a new text input state with the given buffer.\n    pub fn init(backing_buffer: []u8) TextInputState {\n        return .{\n            .buffer = backing_buffer,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Create a text input state with initial content.\n    pub fn initWithContent(backing_buffer: []u8, initial: []const u8) TextInputState {\n        var state = init(backing_buffer);\n        state.setText(initial);\n        return state;\n    }\n\n    /// Get the current text content.\n    pub fn text(self: TextInputState) []const u8 {\n        return self.buffer[0..self.len];\n    }\n\n    /// Set the text content, replacing all existing content.\n    pub fn setText(self: *TextInputState, content: []const u8) void {\n        const max = self.maxLength();\n        const copy_len = @min(content.len, max);\n        @memcpy(self.buffer[0..copy_len], content[0..copy_len]);\n        self.len = copy_len;\n        self.cursor = copy_len;\n        self.anchor = copy_len;\n        self.scroll_offset = 0;\n    }\n\n    /// Clear all content.\n    pub fn clear(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        self.len = 0;\n        self.cursor = 0;\n        self.anchor = 0;\n        self.scroll_offset = 0;\n    }\n\n    /// Get maximum allowed length.\n    fn maxLength(self: TextInputState) usize {\n        if (self.max_len > 0) {\n            return @min(self.max_len, self.buffer.len);\n        }\n        return self.buffer.len;\n    }\n\n    // ========================================\n    // Cursor Movement\n    // ========================================\n\n    /// Move cursor left by one character.\n    pub fn cursorLeft(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        if (self.cursor > 0) {\n            self.cursor = self.prevCharBoundary(self.cursor);\n        }\n        self.anchor = self.cursor;\n    }\n\n    /// Move cursor right by one character.\n    pub fn cursorRight(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        if (self.cursor < self.len) {\n            self.cursor = self.nextCharBoundary(self.cursor);\n        }\n        self.anchor = self.cursor;\n    }\n\n    /// Move cursor to start of line.\n    pub fn cursorHome(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        self.cursor = 0;\n        self.anchor = 0;\n    }\n\n    /// Move cursor to end of line.\n    pub fn cursorEnd(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        self.cursor = self.len;\n        self.anchor = self.len;\n    }\n\n    /// Move cursor left by one word.\n    pub fn cursorWordLeft(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        self.cursor = self.findWordBoundaryLeft(self.cursor);\n        self.anchor = self.cursor;\n    }\n\n    /// Move cursor right by one word.\n    pub fn cursorWordRight(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        self.cursor = self.findWordBoundaryRight(self.cursor);\n        self.anchor = self.cursor;\n    }\n\n    // ========================================\n    // Selection\n    // ========================================\n\n    /// Check if there is an active selection.\n    pub fn hasSelection(self: TextInputState) bool {\n        return self.cursor != self.anchor;\n    }\n\n    /// Get the selection range [start, end).\n    pub fn selectionRange(self: TextInputState) struct { start: usize, end: usize } {\n        return .{\n            .start = @min(self.cursor, self.anchor),\n            .end = @max(self.cursor, self.anchor),\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Get the selected text.\n    pub fn selectedText(self: TextInputState) []const u8 {\n        const range = self.selectionRange();\n        return self.buffer[range.start..range.end];\n    }\n\n    /// Clear selection (keep cursor position).\n    pub fn clearSelection(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        self.anchor = self.cursor;\n    }\n\n    /// Select all text.\n    pub fn selectAll(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        self.anchor = 0;\n        self.cursor = self.len;\n    }\n\n    /// Extend selection left by one character.\n    pub fn selectLeft(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        if (self.cursor > 0) {\n            self.cursor = self.prevCharBoundary(self.cursor);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Extend selection right by one character.\n    pub fn selectRight(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        if (self.cursor < self.len) {\n            self.cursor = self.nextCharBoundary(self.cursor);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Extend selection to start of line.\n    pub fn selectToStart(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        self.cursor = 0;\n    }\n\n    /// Extend selection to end of line.\n    pub fn selectToEnd(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        self.cursor = self.len;\n    }\n\n    /// Extend selection left by one word.\n    pub fn selectWordLeft(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        self.cursor = self.findWordBoundaryLeft(self.cursor);\n    }\n\n    /// Extend selection right by one word.\n    pub fn selectWordRight(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        self.cursor = self.findWordBoundaryRight(self.cursor);\n    }\n\n    // ========================================\n    // Editing\n    // ========================================\n\n    /// Insert a character at cursor position.\n    /// Replaces selection if active.\n    pub fn insertChar(self: *TextInputState, char: u21) void {\n        var utf8_buf: [4]u8 = undefined;\n        const utf8_len = std.unicode.utf8Encode(char, &utf8_buf) catch return;\n        self.insertBytes(utf8_buf[0..utf8_len]);\n    }\n\n    /// Insert text at cursor position.\n    /// Replaces selection if active.\n    pub fn insertBytes(self: *TextInputState, bytes: []const u8) void {\n        // Delete selection first if present\n        if (self.hasSelection()) {\n            self.deleteSelection();\n        }\n\n        const max = self.maxLength();\n        const available = max -| self.len;\n        const insert_len = @min(bytes.len, available);\n        if (insert_len == 0) return;\n\n        // Make room by shifting content after cursor\n        const after_cursor = self.len - self.cursor;\n        if (after_cursor > 0) {\n            std.mem.copyBackwards(\n                u8,\n                self.buffer[self.cursor + insert_len .. self.len + insert_len],\n                self.buffer[self.cursor..self.len],\n            );\n        }\n\n        // Insert new content\n        @memcpy(self.buffer[self.cursor .. self.cursor + insert_len], bytes[0..insert_len]);\n        self.len += insert_len;\n        self.cursor += insert_len;\n        self.anchor = self.cursor;\n    }\n\n    /// Delete character before cursor (backspace).\n    pub fn deleteBackward(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        if (self.hasSelection()) {\n            self.deleteSelection();\n            return;\n        }\n\n        if (self.cursor == 0) return;\n\n        const prev = self.prevCharBoundary(self.cursor);\n        const delete_len = self.cursor - prev;\n\n        // Shift content after cursor\n        const after = self.len - self.cursor;\n        if (after > 0) {\n            std.mem.copyForwards(\n                u8,\n                self.buffer[prev .. prev + after],\n                self.buffer[self.cursor..self.len],\n            );\n        }\n\n        self.len -= delete_len;\n        self.cursor = prev;\n        self.anchor = prev;\n    }\n\n    /// Delete character at cursor (delete key).\n    pub fn deleteForward(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        if (self.hasSelection()) {\n            self.deleteSelection();\n            return;\n        }\n\n        if (self.cursor >= self.len) return;\n\n        const next = self.nextCharBoundary(self.cursor);\n        const delete_len = next - self.cursor;\n\n        // Shift content after deleted character\n        const after = self.len - next;\n        if (after > 0) {\n            std.mem.copyForwards(\n                u8,\n                self.buffer[self.cursor .. self.cursor + after],\n                self.buffer[next..self.len],\n            );\n        }\n\n        self.len -= delete_len;\n    }\n\n    /// Delete word before cursor.\n    pub fn deleteWordBackward(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        if (self.hasSelection()) {\n            self.deleteSelection();\n            return;\n        }\n\n        const target = self.findWordBoundaryLeft(self.cursor);\n        if (target == self.cursor) return;\n\n        const delete_len = self.cursor - target;\n        const after = self.len - self.cursor;\n        if (after > 0) {\n            std.mem.copyForwards(\n                u8,\n                self.buffer[target .. target + after],\n                self.buffer[self.cursor..self.len],\n            );\n        }\n\n        self.len -= delete_len;\n        self.cursor = target;\n        self.anchor = target;\n    }\n\n    /// Delete word after cursor.\n    pub fn deleteWordForward(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        if (self.hasSelection()) {\n            self.deleteSelection();\n            return;\n        }\n\n        const target = self.findWordBoundaryRight(self.cursor);\n        if (target == self.cursor) return;\n\n        const delete_len = target - self.cursor;\n        const after = self.len - target;\n        if (after > 0) {\n            std.mem.copyForwards(\n                u8,\n                self.buffer[self.cursor .. self.cursor + after],\n                self.buffer[target..self.len],\n            );\n        }\n\n        self.len -= delete_len;\n    }\n\n    /// Delete the current selection.\n    fn deleteSelection(self: *TextInputState) void {\n        if (!self.hasSelection()) return;\n\n        const range = self.selectionRange();\n        const delete_len = range.end - range.start;\n        const after = self.len - range.end;\n\n        if (after > 0) {\n            std.mem.copyForwards(\n                u8,\n                self.buffer[range.start .. range.start + after],\n                self.buffer[range.end..self.len],\n            );\n        }\n\n        self.len -= delete_len;\n        self.cursor = range.start;\n        self.anchor = range.start;\n    }\n\n    // ========================================\n    // Clipboard Operations\n    // ========================================\n\n    /// Copy selected text to provided buffer.\n    /// Returns the copied text slice, or empty if no selection.\n    pub fn copyTo(self: TextInputState, dest: []u8) []const u8 {\n        if (!self.hasSelection()) return dest[0..0];\n\n        const selected = self.selectedText();\n        const copy_len = @min(selected.len, dest.len);\n        @memcpy(dest[0..copy_len], selected[0..copy_len]);\n        return dest[0..copy_len];\n    }\n\n    /// Cut selected text to provided buffer.\n    /// Returns the cut text slice, or empty if no selection.\n    pub fn cutTo(self: *TextInputState, dest: []u8) []const u8 {\n        const copied = self.copyTo(dest);\n        if (copied.len > 0) {\n            self.deleteSelection();\n        }\n        return copied;\n    }\n\n    /// Paste text from provided slice.\n    pub fn paste(self: *TextInputState, content: []const u8) void {\n        self.insertBytes(content);\n    }\n\n    // ========================================\n    // Input Handling\n    // ========================================\n\n    /// Handle keyboard input.\n    /// Returns true if the event was handled.\n    pub fn handleKey(self: *TextInputState, key: Key) bool {\n        const ctrl = key.modifiers.ctrl;\n        const shift = key.modifiers.shift;\n\n        switch (key.code) {\n            .char => |c| {\n                if (ctrl) {\n                    // Ctrl+key shortcuts\n                    switch (c) {\n                        'a' => {\n                            self.selectAll();\n                            return true;\n                        },\n                        'w' => {\n                            self.deleteWordBackward();\n                            return true;\n                        },\n                        'u' => {\n                            self.clear();\n                            return true;\n                        },\n                        else => {},\n                    }\n                    return false;\n                }\n                // Regular character input\n                self.insertChar(c);\n                return true;\n            },\n            .left => {\n                if (ctrl and shift) {\n                    self.selectWordLeft();\n                } else if (ctrl) {\n                    self.cursorWordLeft();\n                } else if (shift) {\n                    self.selectLeft();\n                } else {\n                    self.cursorLeft();\n                }\n                return true;\n            },\n            .right => {\n                if (ctrl and shift) {\n                    self.selectWordRight();\n                } else if (ctrl) {\n                    self.cursorWordRight();\n                } else if (shift) {\n                    self.selectRight();\n                } else {\n                    self.cursorRight();\n                }\n                return true;\n            },\n            .home => {\n                if (shift) {\n                    self.selectToStart();\n                } else {\n                    self.cursorHome();\n                }\n                return true;\n            },\n            .end => {\n                if (shift) {\n                    self.selectToEnd();\n                } else {\n                    self.cursorEnd();\n                }\n                return true;\n            },\n            .backspace => {\n                if (ctrl) {\n                    self.deleteWordBackward();\n                } else {\n                    self.deleteBackward();\n                }\n                return true;\n            },\n            .delete => {\n                if (ctrl) {\n                    self.deleteWordForward();\n                } else {\n                    self.deleteForward();\n                }\n                return true;\n            },\n            else => {},\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    // ========================================\n    // UTF-8 Helpers\n    // ========================================\n\n    /// Find the previous character boundary.\n    fn prevCharBoundary(self: TextInputState, pos: usize) usize {\n        if (pos == 0) return 0;\n        var i = pos - 1;\n        while (i > 0 and !isCharStart(self.buffer[i])) {\n            i -= 1;\n        }\n        return i;\n    }\n\n    /// Find the next character boundary.\n    fn nextCharBoundary(self: TextInputState, pos: usize) usize {\n        if (pos >= self.len) return self.len;\n        var i = pos + 1;\n        while (i < self.len and !isCharStart(self.buffer[i])) {\n            i += 1;\n        }\n        return i;\n    }\n\n    /// Check if byte is a UTF-8 character start.\n    fn isCharStart(byte: u8) bool {\n        return (byte & 0xC0) != 0x80;\n    }\n\n    /// Check if character is a word character.\n    fn isWordChar(char: u8) bool {\n        return std.ascii.isAlphanumeric(char) or char == '_';\n    }\n\n    /// Find word boundary to the left.\n    fn findWordBoundaryLeft(self: TextInputState, pos: usize) usize {\n        if (pos == 0) return 0;\n\n        var i = pos;\n\n        // Skip any non-word characters immediately before cursor\n        while (i > 0 and !isWordChar(self.buffer[i - 1])) {\n            i -= 1;\n        }\n\n        // Skip word characters\n        while (i > 0 and isWordChar(self.buffer[i - 1])) {\n            i -= 1;\n        }\n\n        return i;\n    }\n\n    /// Find word boundary to the right.\n    fn findWordBoundaryRight(self: TextInputState, pos: usize) usize {\n        if (pos >= self.len) return self.len;\n\n        var i = pos;\n\n        // Skip word characters at cursor\n        while (i < self.len and isWordChar(self.buffer[i])) {\n            i += 1;\n        }\n\n        // Skip any non-word characters\n        while (i < self.len and !isWordChar(self.buffer[i])) {\n            i += 1;\n        }\n\n        return i;\n    }\n\n    // ========================================\n    // Display Helpers\n    // ========================================\n\n    /// Calculate the display width of text up to a byte position.\n    pub fn displayWidthTo(self: TextInputState, byte_pos: usize) usize {\n        var width: usize = 0;\n        var i: usize = 0;\n        const content = self.buffer[0..@min(byte_pos, self.len)];\n\n        while (i < content.len) {\n            const byte = content[i];\n            if (byte < 0x80) {\n                width += 1;\n                i += 1;\n            } else {\n                const char_len = std.unicode.utf8ByteSequenceLength(byte) catch {\n                    i += 1;\n                    continue;\n                };\n                if (i + char_len <= content.len) {\n                    const codepoint = std.unicode.utf8Decode(content[i..][0..char_len]) catch {\n                        i += 1;\n                        continue;\n                    };\n                    // Rough approximation: CJK and emoji are double-width\n                    if (codepoint >= 0x1100) {\n                        width += 2;\n                    } else {\n                        width += 1;\n                    }\n                }\n                i += char_len;\n            }\n        }\n        return width;\n    }\n\n    /// Update scroll offset to keep cursor visible.\n    pub fn updateScrollOffset(self: *TextInputState, viewport_width: u16) void {\n        if (viewport_width == 0) return;\n\n        const cursor_display_pos = self.displayWidthTo(self.cursor);\n        const vw: usize = viewport_width;\n\n        if (cursor_display_pos < self.scroll_offset) {\n            self.scroll_offset = cursor_display_pos;\n        } else if (cursor_display_pos >= self.scroll_offset + vw) {\n            self.scroll_offset = cursor_display_pos -| (vw -| 1);\n        }\n    }\n};\n\n/// TextInput widget for rendering text input fields.\npub const TextInput = struct {\n    /// Text input state.\n    state: *TextInputState,\n\n    /// Default text style.\n    style: Style = Style.empty,\n\n    /// Cursor style (when focused).\n    cursor_style: Style = Style.init().reverse(),\n\n    /// Selection highlight style.\n    selection_style: Style = Style.init().bg(.blue),\n\n    /// Placeholder text when empty.\n    placeholder: []const u8 = \"\",\n\n    /// Placeholder style.\n    placeholder_style: Style = Style.init().dim(),\n\n    /// Whether the input is focused (shows cursor).\n    focused: bool = true,\n\n    /// Render the text input into the buffer.\n    pub fn render(self: TextInput, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n\n        // Update scroll offset based on viewport\n        self.state.updateScrollOffset(area.width);\n\n        // Fill background\n        buf.fill(area, Cell.styled(' ', self.style));\n\n        const content = self.state.text();\n\n        // Show placeholder if empty and not focused\n        if (content.len == 0 and self.placeholder.len > 0 and !self.focused) {\n            buf.setString(area.x, area.y, self.placeholder, self.placeholder_style);\n            return;\n        }\n\n        // Render visible text\n        const selection = self.state.selectionRange();\n        const scroll = self.state.scroll_offset;\n\n        var x: u16 = area.x;\n        var byte_idx: usize = 0;\n        var display_idx: usize = 0;\n\n        while (byte_idx < content.len and x < area.right()) {\n            const byte = content[byte_idx];\n            const char_len = if (byte < 0x80)\n                @as(usize, 1)\n            else\n                std.unicode.utf8ByteSequenceLength(byte) catch 1;\n\n            if (byte_idx + char_len > content.len) break;\n\n            const codepoint = if (byte < 0x80)\n                @as(u21, byte)\n            else\n                std.unicode.utf8Decode(content[byte_idx..][0..char_len]) catch byte;\n\n            // Rough display width\n            const char_width: usize = if (codepoint >= 0x1100) 2 else 1;\n\n            // Check if this character is visible\n            if (display_idx + char_width > scroll) {\n                // Determine style\n                var char_style = self.style;\n                const in_selection = self.state.hasSelection() and\n                    byte_idx >= selection.start and byte_idx < selection.end;\n\n                if (in_selection) {\n                    char_style = self.selection_style;\n                }\n\n                // Draw cursor\n                if (self.focused and byte_idx == self.state.cursor) {\n                    char_style = self.cursor_style;\n                }\n\n                buf.set(x, area.y, Cell.styled(codepoint, char_style));\n                x += @intCast(@min(char_width, area.right() - x));\n            }\n\n            display_idx += char_width;\n            byte_idx += char_len;\n        }\n\n        // Draw cursor at end if needed\n        if (self.focused and self.state.cursor >= self.state.len) {\n            if (x < area.right()) {\n                buf.set(x, area.y, Cell.styled(' ', self.cursor_style));\n            }\n        }\n    }\n};\n\n// ============================================================\n// SANITY TESTS - TextInputState basic functionality\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"sanity: TextInputState default values\" {\n    var backing: [256]u8 = undefined;\n    const state = TextInputState.init(&backing);\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), state.len);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), state.cursor);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), state.anchor);\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"\", state.text());\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: TextInputState.initWithContent\" {\n    var backing: [256]u8 = undefined;\n    const state = TextInputState.initWithContent(&backing, \"hello\");\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 5), state.len);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 5), state.cursor);\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"hello\", state.text());\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: TextInputState.setText\" {\n    var backing: [256]u8 = undefined;\n    var state = TextInputState.init(&backing);\n\n    state.setText(\"world\");\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"world\", state.text());\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 5), state.cursor);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: TextInputState.clear\" {\n    var backing: [256]u8 = undefined;\n    var state = TextInputState.initWithContent(&backing, \"test\");\n\n    state.clear();\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"\", state.text());\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), state.cursor);\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// BEHAVIOR TESTS - Cursor Movement\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"behavior: TextInputState cursor left/right\" {\n    var backing: [256]u8 = undefined;\n    var state = TextInputState.initWithContent(&backing, \"hello\");\n\n    state.cursorLeft();\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 4), state.cursor);\n\n    state.cursorRight();\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 5), state.cursor);\n\n    state.cursorHome();\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), state.cursor);\n\n    state.cursorEnd();\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 5), state.cursor);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: TextInputState cursor word navigation\" {\n    var backing: [256]u8 = undefined;\n    var state = TextInputState.initWithContent(&backing, \"hello world foo\");\n\n    state.cursorHome();\n    state.cursorWordRight();\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 6), state.cursor);\n\n    state.cursorWordRight();\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 12), state.cursor);\n\n    state.cursorWordLeft();\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 6), state.cursor);\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// BEHAVIOR TESTS - Selection\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"behavior: TextInputState selection\" {\n    var backing: [256]u8 = undefined;\n    var state = TextInputState.initWithContent(&backing, \"hello world\");\n    state.cursorHome();\n\n    try std.testing.expect(!state.hasSelection());\n\n    state.selectRight();\n    state.selectRight();\n    state.selectRight();\n\n    try std.testing.expect(state.hasSelection());\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"hel\", state.selectedText());\n\n    const range = state.selectionRange();\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), range.start);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 3), range.end);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: TextInputState selectAll\" {\n    var backing: [256]u8 = undefined;\n    var state = TextInputState.initWithContent(&backing, \"hello\");\n\n    state.selectAll();\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"hello\", state.selectedText());\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// BEHAVIOR TESTS - Editing\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"behavior: TextInputState insertChar\" {\n    var backing: [256]u8 = undefined;\n    var state = TextInputState.init(&backing);\n\n    state.insertChar('a');\n    state.insertChar('b');\n    state.insertChar('c');\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"abc\", state.text());\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 3), state.cursor);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: TextInputState insertBytes\" {\n    var backing: [256]u8 = undefined;\n    var state = TextInputState.initWithContent(&backing, \"hello\");\n    state.cursor = 5;\n\n    state.insertBytes(\" world\");\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"hello world\", state.text());\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: TextInputState insert replaces selection\" {\n    var backing: [256]u8 = undefined;\n    var state = TextInputState.initWithContent(&backing, \"hello world\");\n    state.cursorHome();\n\n    // Select \"hello\"\n    state.anchor = 0;\n    state.cursor = 5;\n\n    state.insertBytes(\"hi\");\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"hi world\", state.text());\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: TextInputState deleteBackward\" {\n    var backing: [256]u8 = undefined;\n    var state = TextInputState.initWithContent(&backing, \"hello\");\n\n    state.deleteBackward();\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"hell\", state.text());\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 4), state.cursor);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: TextInputState deleteForward\" {\n    var backing: [256]u8 = undefined;\n    var state = TextInputState.initWithContent(&backing, \"hello\");\n    state.cursorHome();\n\n    state.deleteForward();\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"ello\", state.text());\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), state.cursor);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: TextInputState deleteWordBackward\" {\n    var backing: [256]u8 = undefined;\n    var state = TextInputState.initWithContent(&backing, \"hello world\");\n\n    state.deleteWordBackward();\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"hello \", state.text());\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// BEHAVIOR TESTS - Clipboard\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"behavior: TextInputState copyTo\" {\n    var backing: [256]u8 = undefined;\n    var state = TextInputState.initWithContent(&backing, \"hello world\");\n    state.anchor = 0;\n    state.cursor = 5;\n\n    var clip_buf: [256]u8 = undefined;\n    const copied = state.copyTo(&clip_buf);\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"hello\", copied);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: TextInputState cutTo\" {\n    var backing: [256]u8 = undefined;\n    var state = TextInputState.initWithContent(&backing, \"hello world\");\n    state.anchor = 0;\n    state.cursor = 6;\n\n    var clip_buf: [256]u8 = undefined;\n    const cut = state.cutTo(&clip_buf);\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"hello \", cut);\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"world\", state.text());\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: TextInputState paste\" {\n    var backing: [256]u8 = undefined;\n    var state = TextInputState.initWithContent(&backing, \"hello\");\n\n    state.paste(\" world\");\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"hello world\", state.text());\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// BEHAVIOR TESTS - Input Handling\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"behavior: TextInputState handleKey character input\" {\n    var backing: [256]u8 = undefined;\n    var state = TextInputState.init(&backing);\n\n    const handled = state.handleKey(.{ .code = .{ .char = 'x' } });\n    try std.testing.expect(handled);\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"x\", state.text());\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: TextInputState handleKey navigation\" {\n    var backing: [256]u8 = undefined;\n    var state = TextInputState.initWithContent(&backing, \"test\");\n\n    _ = state.handleKey(.{ .code = .left });\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 3), state.cursor);\n\n    _ = state.handleKey(.{ .code = .home });\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), state.cursor);\n\n    _ = state.handleKey(.{ .code = .end });\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 4), state.cursor);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: TextInputState handleKey with shift selects\" {\n    var backing: [256]u8 = undefined;\n    var state = TextInputState.initWithContent(&backing, \"test\");\n    state.cursorHome();\n\n    _ = state.handleKey(.{ .code = .right, .modifiers = .{ .shift = true } });\n    _ = state.handleKey(.{ .code = .right, .modifiers = .{ .shift = true } });\n\n    try std.testing.expect(state.hasSelection());\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"te\", state.selectedText());\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: TextInputState handleKey Ctrl+A selects all\" {\n    var backing: [256]u8 = undefined;\n    var state = TextInputState.initWithContent(&backing, \"hello\");\n\n    _ = state.handleKey(.{ .code = .{ .char = 'a' }, .modifiers = .{ .ctrl = true } });\n\n    try std.testing.expect(state.hasSelection());\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"hello\", state.selectedText());\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// BEHAVIOR TESTS - Rendering\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"behavior: TextInput renders text\" {\n    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 1);\n    defer buf.deinit();\n\n    var backing: [256]u8 = undefined;\n    var state = TextInputState.initWithContent(&backing, \"hello\");\n\n    const input = TextInput{\n        .state = &state,\n        .focused = false,\n    };\n    input.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 20, 1), &buf);\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'h'), buf.get(0, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'e'), buf.get(1, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'l'), buf.get(2, 0).char);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: TextInput renders cursor when focused\" {\n    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 1);\n    defer buf.deinit();\n\n    var backing: [256]u8 = undefined;\n    var state = TextInputState.initWithContent(&backing, \"hi\");\n    state.cursor = 2;\n\n    const input = TextInput{\n        .state = &state,\n        .focused = true,\n        .cursor_style = Style.init().reverse(),\n    };\n    input.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 20, 1), &buf);\n\n    // Cursor at position 2 should have cursor style\n    try std.testing.expect(buf.get(2, 0).style.hasAttribute(.reverse));\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: TextInput renders placeholder when empty\" {\n    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 1);\n
